> **REPO & VERSION CONTEXT (read first):** You audit **CRM2 (v2)** — a GREENFIELD rebuild living in `crm2/`, which has its **OWN git repo** (`github.com/acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`) even though it sits INSIDE the v1 monorepo directory `CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD/` (v1 git-ignores it). **THREE separate git repos share that one folder:**
> 1. **v1 (legacy, in prod)** — repo `acsdeveloper2025/CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD`; the live app = `CRM-BACKEND/` + `CRM-FRONTEND/`. ⚠️ `acs_db_final_version.sql` at the v1 root is the **v1** schema — NEVER audit v2 against it; the v2 schema is `crm2/db/v2/migrations/` (+ the live test/dev DBs).
> 2. **v2 (this, greenfield build)** — repo `acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`; everything you review is here under `crm2/`.
> 3. **mobile (field-executive app)** — `crm-mobile-native/`, repo `acsdeveloper2025/crm-mobile-native`, React-Native, **ALREADY DEVELOPED & currently CONNECTED TO v1** (`https://crm.allcheckservices.com/api/mobile`). It is a first-class `/api/v2` consumer to be rebased onto v2 later (`crm2/MOBILE_API_COMPATIBILITY_MATRIX.md`) — **never break the mobile contract** (ADR-0012).

# Ledger — CEO / Quality-Sentinel

Charter: AGENT_ORG.md row 1. Product fit · scope discipline · ALL frozen-standard conformance ·
bugs/risks · final BLOCK. Read this before each audit; append after.

## Standing watch-list
- Scope creep (Karpathy): every changed line must trace to the slice's request.
- Frozen standards: Responsive-First · OCC ADR-0019 · color/uppercase tokens · pagination/DataGrid ·
  import/export · effective-from · RBAC default-deny · append-only audit · repository/layering.
- "Green build that breaks at runtime" — watch for contract changes whose consumers weren't updated
  (tsc passes through unchecked casts; the harness can pass during the loading window). See DataGrid slice.

## Log
- **2026-06-16 — Slice 2c-2 device FIELD-PHOTO upload (`cbc9d0d`, ADR-0034, committed + previously panel-audited) + backend task REVOKE re-add (ADR-0033 Correction 2026-06-16, WORKING-TREE uncommitted). FINAL VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit the revoke diff).** Re-audited both adversarially; `pnpm verify` green (api 619) + live E2E/browser per the build, not re-run.
  - **(B) Revoke — product logic CORRECT.** `revokeTaskInPlace` (renamed from `revokeTaskByDevice`, repository.ts:1115) UPDATEs only `status IN ('ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS')`; on 0-rows it re-reads → not-found 404 / REVOKED idempotent-200 / else 409 INVALID_TRANSITION — so COMPLETED **and** PENDING are blocked (409), ASSIGNED/IN_PROGRESS allowed, exactly the owner's corrected rule. Shared by device (ownership-bound, verification-tasks/service.ts:111) and office (scope-bound, cases/service.ts:355 via `taskAssignmentState` → out-of-scope null → 404 IDOR-safe). Reason mandatory (`RevokeTaskSchema` min(1), MAX_REMARK — token, no magic number). No OCC version on revoke — consistent with the device path. Test (cases.api.test.ts:1226) covers reason-400 / KYC_VERIFIER-403 / out-of-scope-MANAGER-404 / 200+REVOKED+remark / idempotent-200 / COMPLETED-409. Perms: TASK_REVOKE granted MANAGER+BACKEND_USER (permissions.ts:85,108), TEAM_LEADER/KYC_VERIFIER/FIELD_AGENT correctly excluded; mig 0056 mirrors the role grant (BACKEND_USER+MANAGER) + ON CONFLICT idempotent. FE: REVOCABLE=Set(['ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS']), gated `canRevoke`, ReasonForm generalized (required) — surgical, theme-tokens only (text-destructive/border-border/bg-surface-muted), mutual-exclusive row state handled.
  - **(A) Photo upload — re-confirmed, no regression.** Idempotent by operation id (pre-check `fieldAttachmentsByOperation` → replay 200 cached, NOT re-store; concurrent UNIQUE_VIOLATION race → return winner; never 409-as-success). Server hash = sha256(stripped) evidence; client hash regex-validated then compared to sha256(received bytes) (correct transit check, pre-strip), mismatch logged-not-rejected. EXIF/GPS stripped via re-encode w/o withMetadata + auto-orient (photo.ts:30); bounds 15 MiB/10 files/50 MP all named consts. Per-file→failed[], only STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED 503 fails the request. Mig 0055 kind-discriminator default backfills office rows, partial-UNIQUE op_id, triple-write note present.
  - **Frozen standards — respected.** Tokens-only (FE), UPPERCASE statuses, named constants (MAX_REMARK/MAX_FIELD_PHOTO_BYTES/MAX_FIELD_PHOTOS/THUMB_PX), RBAC default-deny (new perm, explicit grants), append-only audit (revoke appends UPDATE row), scope-guard reused (no new IDOR path), repository/layering intact. No scope creep — every changed line traces to (A) or (B).
  - **Disposition of OPEN/stale items (all cosmetic, NON-BLOCKING):** (1) ADR-0033 body lines 28 & 96 still read "backend NEVER revokes / Removed entirely" — but the Correction header (line 17) **explicitly supersedes them by pointer** (ADR-as-amendment convention, history not rewritten). Acceptable; leave as-is. (2) "device-REVOKED" wording in reassign comments (cases/controller.ts:226, service.ts:378, sdk/client.ts:549, CaseDetailPage.tsx:359) is now incompletely descriptive — a task can be office-REVOKED too — but reassign-after-revoke is status-based (REASSIGNABLE=Set(['REVOKED'])), not origin-based, so the **logic is correct**; only the word "device-" is stale. (3) permissions.ts:3 doc-comment says "6 roles" while 7 are defined (incl KYC_VERIFIER) — **pre-existing**, not introduced here, surgical-rule leave. (4) `fieldAttachmentsByOperation` uses `split_part(...)` non-sargable predicate — negligible at device scale, pre-existing committed code. None are shipping bugs or frozen-decision violations.

- **2026-06-06 · DataGrid server-pagination Slice 2 — `locations` (157k pincode catalog) list → `Paginated<T>`
  + Universal DataGrid + NEW migration `0020_locations_search_indexes.sql` (working tree, pre-commit)** —
  **VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit).** All 5 specialists (DB/Perf/Principal/API-Contract/Design) PASS; I
  re-verified independently and ran the gate + EXPLAIN myself rather than rubber-stamping.
  - **🎯 The Slice-1 index RATCHET is RESOLVED for locations.** This slice was the HARD GATE I handed DB/Perf.
    Migration `0020` adds: 4× pg_trgm GIN (pincode/area/city/state) backing the global leading-wildcard ILIKE
    search; `idx_locations_pincode_sort (pincode,id)` backing the default `ORDER BY pincode,id` over ALL rows
    (the pre-existing `idx_locations_pincode WHERE is_active` partial does NOT cover the unfiltered admin list).
    `effective_from` already indexed (0015). **Forward-only + idempotent CONFIRMED** — re-ran 0020 against the
    live 157k DB: every object `IF NOT EXISTS`/`CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS` skipped cleanly, no error.
  - **Triple-write CONFIRMED on BOTH DBs.** Dev `crm2_dev`@:54329 (157,072 rows — the real all-India catalog)
    AND test `crm2_test`@:5433 both carry all 5 new indexes (`pg_indexes` enumerated on each). Note: dev DB
    is named `crm2_dev` on :54329 (not `crm2`); both verified directly. Not source-only → dev API won't 500.
  - **EXPLAIN ANALYZE on the live 157k catalog (hard numbers, <2s budget):** default list (pincode, page 1) =
    **0.16 ms** (Index Scan `idx_locations_pincode_sort`, no sort node); deep OFFSET 150k on default sort = 41 ms;
    search ILIKE '%mumbai%' = planner walks the ordered pincode idx + filters (cost 552, NOT a 157k seq scan —
    the trgm GINs back selective/count paths). **Residual:** 8 of 9 sortable cols (area/city/state/country/
    createdAt/updatedAt — pincode+effective_from ARE indexed) fall to parallel-seq-scan + top-N heapsort.
    MEASURED worst case = sort by city + deep OFFSET 150k = **180 ms**; page-1 unindexed sort = 28-41 ms. Two
    orders of magnitude under the 2s budget at 157k. **Disposition: ACCEPTABLE — ratchet RESOLVED, not deferred.**
    The migration indexed the access paths that would actually seq-scan (default sort + search); top-N sort on a
    non-default column is cheap and proportionate (Karpathy — not gold-plating a 9-index migration). RATCHET
    NARROWED, not dropped: if `cases`/another 157k+ table sorts on a non-default column under real load, re-measure;
    if locations ever 10×s, add covering sort indexes on the hot sort columns.
  - **Array→envelope trap (#1 standing watch + CLAUDE.md DON'T-REGRESS) — CLOSED for this slice.** Grepped all
    web+sdk: every `/api/v2/locations` LIST read now `Paginated<Location>` + `.items` — LocationsPage DataGrid

      bulk actions · keyboard navigation incl. clickable-row keyboard parity) — DEFERRED per DATAGRID_STANDARD §2.
    - **CPV** remains bespoke (master-detail accordion; DataGrid core has no row-expansion) — tracked separately, out of
      this rollout's scope.
  - **🏁 ROLLOUT COMPLETE.** All 6 admin/operational lists migrated to `Paginated<T>` + Universal DataGrid: Users · VU ·
    Templates (C-2..C-4 Slice 1) · Locations (Slice 2) · Cases (Slice 3) · Rates (Slice 4) + the clients/products
    reference. No list endpoint remains on the legacy array shape. **Cleared to commit.**

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 1A — `0021_cases_growth_indexes.sql` (migration-ONLY, cases-growth ratchet tail). VERDICT: PASS
  (clear to commit).** This is the rollout tail that resolves the cases-growth index ratchet I carried out of Slice 3
  (registry Section C / B-2). Re-verified independently against the live cases-list query rather than rubber-stamping.
  - **Serves the registry item — no scope creep.** 4 additive `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` + `CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT
    EXISTS pg_trgm`. Zero app code, zero schema/column/constraint/data change. Every changed line traces to a cases-list
    access path: default-sort composite (`created_at DESC, id DESC` = CASE_PAGE_SPEC.defaultSort), the `products` FK join,
    and the two leading-wildcard ILIKE search columns (`case_number`, `pa.name`). Karpathy-clean — it indexes the paths
    that would seq-scan as cases accumulate, nothing more.
  - **No frozen-standard violation.** Mirrors the 0020 migration idiom exactly (header rationale + trgm-GIN-per-search-col
    + composite sort index); forward-only + idempotent (every object `IF NOT EXISTS`); migrations stay the only place raw
    DDL lives. No DataGrid/OCC/RBAC/audit/contract surface touched (it's purely a planner optimization).
  - **Disposition story is HONEST and recorded.** (a) `count(*) OVER()` — WONTFIX confirmed: the list uses a *separate*
    non-windowed `count(*)::int` COUNT query (repo.ts:225), so there is no window-function path to index; the migration
    correctly does not pretend to address it. (b) small-table sort-index RATCHET — the only sortable columns left
    unindexed are non-default (caseNumber/status/client/etc.); status+client already have 0010 b-trees, the rest fall to
    cheap top-N heapsort at current volume — consistent with the locations(157k) measured-acceptable precedent, carried as
    a re-measure trigger, not a gap. (c) the per-row applicant_count/task_count scalar subselects (the "LATERAL counts"
    ratchet) are deliberately left for a later slice — correctly NOT in scope here.
  - **Risk: LOW.** Additive indexes only; idempotent re-run proven; triple-write done (file + dev :54329/crm2_dev + test
    :5433/crm2_test); chain 0001→0021 clean on fresh DB ×2; `pnpm verify` green (FULL TURBO cache — expected, no code
    inputs changed for a migration-only slice; the figure is honestly caveated). No consumer/contract exposure (DDL-only),
    so the array→envelope #1-watch does not apply.
  - **OPEN (carried, unchanged):** B-22 dropdown limit=200; e2e crash-guard path list across envelope pages; LATERAL
    per-row count subselects (scale-gated, DB+Perf own); non-default-sort re-measure trigger. None blocking.
  - **Cleared to commit. Cases-growth ratchet RESOLVED.**

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 1B — B-22 lightweight `/options` endpoints (working tree, pre-commit; new file `packages/sdk/src/options.ts`).
  VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit).** This RESOLVES the B-22 dropdown-truncation item I've carried across every DataGrid slice.
  Re-audited independently against `git diff` + ran the SDK gate myself rather than rubber-stamp.
  - **🎯 B-22 ratchet CLOSED.** The old feeders did `?active=true&limit=200`+`.items` on genuinely-unbounded master-data
    dropdowns — a silent-truncation timebomb past 200 rows. New unpaginated `GET /{clients,products,verification-units}/options`
    → flat `Option{id,code,name}`; `/users/options` → `UserOption{id,username,name,role}`; VU adds `kind`. All 9 FE feeder call
    sites (CaseCreate ×2, CPV ×3, RateMgmt ×3, UsersPage ×1) flipped to the `/options` reads. No truncation path remains.
  - **Scope — DISCIPLINED, not creep (the CTO's self-flagged question, judged).** The two beyond-literal-B-22 additions are
    both justified and in-class: (a) `users.options()` is the SAME silent-truncation bug class on the reports-to picker
    (`UsersPage.tsx:184` was `?limit=200`→`.items`) — refusing to fix it while fixing its siblings would be arbitrary; (b) VU
    `kind` is a genuine consumer need — RateMgmt already filters units by kind, and `Option` would have dropped it forcing a
    second round-trip. Both trace to the slice's intent (kill dropdown truncation on unbounded master-data feeds). The RateMgmt
    `locations?pincode=&limit=200` + `/pincodes?q=` feeders are CORRECTLY LEFT — bounded per-pincode (dozens « 200), different
    shape; carried as a registry note, not silently swept in. This is the opposite of creep: the boundary was drawn and stated.
  - **Array→envelope trap (#1 standing watch) — inverted but clean.** This slice moves FROM the envelope BACK to a flat array
    on these reads — the exact runtime-cast hazard. Verified every one of the 9 call sites changed the `api<…>` type-arg in
    lockstep with the URL: `api<Option[]>`/`api<VerificationUnitOption[]>`/`api<UserOption[]>` — none left as `Paginated<X>`
    reading `.items` off a now-flat response (that would `undefined.items`→crash). CaseCreate's local `interface Option{id,code,name}`
    is byte-identical to SDK `Option` so its cast is sound. SDK leaf types align with the server SELECT lists exactly.
  - **RBAC default-deny — provably identical to the shipped lists.** Each `/options` route reuses the EXACT `authorize(PERMISSIONS.X)`
    of its sibling list: MASTERDATA_VIEW (clients/products/VU), USER_VIEW (users). No new authz surface. Tests assert it live:
    BE reads master-data options 200 but is DENIED users/options 403 (USER_VIEW=page.users, which BE lacks), 401 unauth on all four.
  - **ADR-0017 (USABLE = active AND in-effect) honored in every options query** — `WHERE is_active AND effective_from <= now()`,
    test-proven per module (inactive + future-dated both excluded; trimmed-shape key assertion). VU keeps `ORDER BY sort_order, name`.
  - **Param-capture trap avoided & commented** — `/options` registered BEFORE `/:id` in all 4 routers (would've been captured as
    id="options"→ NaN/500). users has no GET `/:id` but ordering kept consistent anyway. Correct.
  - **Layering / standards — clean.** controller→service→repo, raw SQL only in repo; no `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in added
    source (grep of `^+` non-test lines = NONE); `options.ts` is a pure `export interface` (0% coverage is expected, no executable
    lines, does NOT threaten thresholds — confirmed by green run). No new pattern/package (no ADR needed). Surgical: +293/-42, every
    file traces to the feeder swap.
  - **Gate (ran SDK myself):** `@crm2/sdk` **63/63 PASS** incl. the load-bearing call-count `toBe(66)` (was 62 + 4 options methods)
    and the new `/options`-URL/GET/no-body assertion. CTO reports `pnpm verify` green (api 200 [+8], web build) + browser-verified
    on /cases/new (Client/Product populate via /options; VU returns id/code/name/kind live). Accepted on the recorded evidence.
  - **OPEN (carried):** RateMgmt `locations?pincode=&limit=200` + `/pincodes?q=` feeders (bounded, registry NOTE not gap);
    e2e crash-guard path list (now also wants the 9 flat-array reads, but they're correct-by-inspection + SDK-tested); non-default-sort
    re-measure trigger. None blocking.
  - **Cleared to commit. B-22 RESOLVED.**

- **2026-06-06 — Server-side column-filter contract (backend-only; working tree, pre-commit).
  VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit).** Generic per-column filtering on the list contract: `pagination.ts`
  gains `FilterField`/`PageSpec.filterMap`/`AppliedFilter`/`resolveFilters()`; clients+products declare
  `filterMap` (code/name text), echo `f_<field>` into envelope `filters`; repos append whitelisted
  `col ILIKE|= $n` with bound values. Realizes DATAGRID_STANDARD §6 (column search) / §8 (multi-column AND).
  - **KEY QUESTION — "contract-first, UI-next": ACCEPTABLE, not a dead feature.** The grid per-column filter UI
    is the explicitly-planned NEXT sub-slice (mirrors how the sort contract preceded its header-click UI). This
    is NOT speculative: it's fully reachable TODAY — `pageQueryToParams` already serializes `filters:{f_code}`
    → `?f_code=hd` (`packages/sdk/src/pagination.ts:44`), so the SDK exercises the path now; it's tested
    (5 unit + 2 api); and it mirrors the proven `sortMap` whitelist line-for-line. The lever lands one slice
    ahead of its handle by design, not orphaned. Decision: in-scope.
  - **Scope — DISCIPLINED.** Touches only `platform/pagination.ts` + clients/products (service+repo+tests).
    Products mirrors clients faithfully (verified: repo filter block byte-identical except the table name).
    No other module touched; no UI; no SDK type churn.
  - **Security — the load-bearing invariant HOLDS.** "column safe to interpolate" is true because
    `AppliedFilter.column` is sourced EXCLUSIVELY from the service's hardcoded `filterMap[field].column`
    (`pagination.ts:69`), never from request data. The request only (a) selects WHICH whitelisted field via the
    `f_` key — membership-gated by `Object.entries(spec.filterMap)` — and (b) supplies `value`, always bound as
    `$n`. Injection test (`f_secret`, `f_is_active=true;DROP`) lands on non-whitelisted fields → dropped; enum
    out-of-set → dropped. No string-concat of any request-controlled token reaches SQL.
  - **OPEN (carried, unchanged):** B-22 bounded feeders; non-default-sort re-measure trigger; saved-views store.
    NEW carried note: the per-column-filter grid UI must actually consume this next slice (else it WOULD become
    dead — track until landed). None blocking. **Cleared to commit.**

    `effective_from` — `client_id`/`product_id` (CP) and `client_product_id`/`verification_unit_id` (CPV) are never in any
    SET clause; the Zod `UpdateClientProductSchema`/`UpdateCpvUnitSchema` accept `{ effectiveFrom }` ONLY (cpv.ts:71-72), so a
    key can't even be smuggled in the body. The "code/keys immutable" frozen decision is intact — reschedule is purely a date
    move, exactly like the blessed clients/products precedent. Honest: the dialog copy states it ("The client/product/unit keys

    ConflictDialog itself — uses the semantic `bg-foreground/40`.** `bg-black` is a raw Tailwind palette color, NOT an

  - **Gate accepted on recorded evidence** (pnpm verify green; api 217 incl. the new reschedule api-test; sdk 63 with the
    call-count bumped 66→68 for the two new `update` methods; browser screenshot of the prefilled "RESCHEDULE HDFC · CAR_LOAN"
    dialog with the immutable-keys note). **Cleared to commit. The one CPV master-data edit gap is CLOSED; ADR-0001 not reopened.**

- **2026-06-06 — ADR-0020 "correctable identity keys while unreferenced" (working tree, pre-commit; new
  `docs/adr/ADR-0020-…md` + clients/products {repository,service,api-test}, shared `MasterDataCrud.tsx`, sdk
  clients/products {schema,test}). VERDICT: FLAG (clear to commit AFTER widening the dependents check — non-blocking
  for the owner's stated typo-fix use case, but the ADR's lock guarantee is under-enforced today).** Audited the diff
  adversarially against the ADR text and the live FK graph in `acs_db_final_version.sql`; re-derived the dependents set
  myself rather than trust the 3-table EXISTS.
  - **GOVERNANCE — ADR-0020 is properly written and correctly amends (not abandons) ADR-0001.** Status Accepted; full
    Context/Decision/Consequences/Alternatives/Related; explicit `Amends: ADR-0001` header + the closing sentence "a key
    that is *in use* is still immutable; only a fresh, unreferenced entry can be corrected." In-use keys stay immutable —
    the frozen guarantee is narrowed, not dropped. The FK-by-surrogate-id rationale (no DB integrity risk; immutability is
    a *business/reporting* guarantee that only bites once referenced) is sound and matches the schema (all FKs are
    `REFERENCES …(id)`, never by code). `users.username` correctly noted as no-FK-deps (login rename, uniqueness-checked,
    no dependents gate). Reopening a frozen ADR via a new superseding-amendment ADR (not by editing ADR-0001 in place) is
    the correct governance move. APPROVED as a governance artifact.
  - **🚩 GOVERNANCE/CORRECTNESS FLAG — the implementation does NOT match the ADR's own scope of "referenced."**
    ADR-0020 defines locked as "referenced by dependent records **or reported on**" and its Context lists report_templates
    among the identity-key entities. But `hasDependents` checks only **3** of the **15** tables that FK to `clients.id`
    (`client_products`, `rates`, `cases` — repository.ts:105-107) and **3** of the **11** FK→`products.id`. MISSING and
    populated-in-schema: `report_templates`, `kyc_rates`, `case_data_templates`, `commission_calculations`,
    `field_user_commission_assignments`, `rate_type_assignments`, `user_client_assignments`/`user_product_assignments`,
    `client_contacts`, `invoices`/`invoice_items`/`invoice_item_tasks`, `szr` (all verified present via `CREATE TABLE` +
    `FK CONSTRAINT … REFERENCES public.clients(id)`/`products(id)`). Consequence: a client/product referenced ONLY by, e.g.,
    a report_template, an invoice, a user-client RBAC assignment, or a commission row — but not by CPV-link/rate/case — passes
    `hasDependents()===false` and its code is editable. That breaks the ADR's *reporting/history-coherence* promise for the
    two most coherence-sensitive tables (report_templates, invoices), which are the ones left unchecked. No data corruption
    (FK by id), but the lock is a partial subset of "in use." **SHOULD-FIX before broad reliance: widen `hasDependents` to the
    full referencing set (or document explicitly in the ADR why only the C→P→case spine counts as "in use").** Non-blocking
    for the immediate owner ask only because prod has 0 report_templates/0 invoices today (per the simplification audit) — so
    the realistic typo-fix-on-a-fresh-row path is safe NOW; the gap is latent.
  - **Scope discipline — exemplary and matches the ADR's stated rollout plan.** `git diff --stat` = exactly clients+products
    (×{repo,service,api-test}) + the shared `MasterDataCrud` + sdk clients/products schema/test; 11 files, +217/-69. VU,
    locations, templates, users.username rollout is explicitly deferred in the ADR — a legitimate reference-then-rollout, NOT
    a "finish 100%" violation: this is a frozen-ADR amendment whose reference impl proves the pattern on the two simplest
    entities before fanning out. Acceptable as P-of-N, provided the follow-ups are tracked.
  - **STALE-DOC nit (non-blocking, Principal-owned too):** both service file-headers still read "`code` is immutable (update
    accepts `name` only)" — clients/service.ts:28 and products/service.ts (header block) — directly contradicting the code 45
    lines below. Pre-existing comment, not touched by the diff, now false. Tidy on next touch.
  - **Gate accepted on recorded evidence** (pnpm verify green; api 220 incl. the new unreferenced-fix + referenced-409 tests;
    sdk 63; live HDFC code-change→409 CODE_LOCKED + name-only→200; browser editable code field + helper). **VERDICT: FLAG —
    clear to commit; widen the dependents check (or amend the ADR's "in use" definition) before the rollout to the other
    master-data entities, since each carries the same partial-subset risk.**

- **2026-06-09 — Keyboard-nav / focus-management a11y slice (working tree, pre-commit; NEW `apps/web/src/lib/useFocusTrap.ts`
  + 3 DataGrid popovers + 8 modal-dialog files + 2 e2e tests). VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit AFTER one pre-commit gate — the new
  hook file is UNTRACKED). Closes the carried-OPEN menu focus-trap/return-focus / keyboard-nav item (DATAGRID_STANDARD §19/§20; axe
  gate 29).** Audited the diff adversarially; enumerated every `bg-foreground/40`/`role=dialog`/`role=menu` surface myself + ran web
  tsc + eslint on the touched files rather than rubber-stamp.
  - **🎯 "Finish one thing to 100%" — VERIFIED COMPLETE, no missed surface.** Enumerated ALL overlays under `apps/web/src`:
    9 `bg-foreground/40` modal overlays (RateMgmt ReviseDialog:571 + HistoryDialog:643, LocationsPage:292, UsersPage:235,
    VerificationUnitDialog:106, CpvPage:34, TemplatesPage:226, ConflictDialog:33, MasterDataCrud:228) + the 3 DataGrid menus
    (Export:313, Columns:381, ColumnFilterSelect:673) — **every one is wired to `useFocusTrap`** (grep-confirmed each `ref=` lands on
    the panel/menu container). `grep role="dialog"` = exactly those 8 files + the carve-out. NO modal dialog or DataGrid menu was
    missed. The only uncovered `bg-foreground/40` is `Layout.tsx:106` — the declared carve-out.
  - **Carve-out (mobile nav drawer) — JUSTIFIED, an honest boundary cut not a half-done rollout.** `Layout.tsx:112` `<aside>` is ONE
    element in BOTH modes (`open` → fixed overlay below lg, `lg:static` in-flow on desktop); it carries NO `role="dialog"` (correct —
    on desktop it isn't a dialog). A trap keyed on `open` would trap keyboard focus inside the always-present desktop sidebar — a real
    WCAG regression. Excluding it until the drawer's `open` is made lg-only-aware is the correct call. Stated in the slice, deferred.
  - **ConflictDialog nested-trap — correct, and the only behavioral subtlety.** ConflictDialog renders as a SIBLING inside the parent
    dialog's outer overlay div (e.g. UsersPage.tsx:320-335, outside the `ref={dialogRef}` panel). Both traps are active at once, but the
    keydown listener is attached to **each panel container** (not document), and the parent panel does NOT contain the ConflictDialog
    panel → Tab/Escape from ConflictDialog fire only on ConflictDialog's listener; no double-handling. On open the inner trap grabs
    focus; on unmount its cleanup restores focus into the parent panel. The parent's `[active]`-dep effect does not re-run, so it never
    fights for focus. Sound. `onEscape=() => undefined` on ConflictDialog makes Escape a deliberate no-op (must-decide dialog) — Tab
    still cycles to Reload/Discard, so NOT a keyboard trap (WCAG 2.1.2 must-have-an-exit is met by the two buttons); the in-code comment
    (ConflictDialog.tsx:28-30) documents exactly this. Honest.
  - **Escape semantics change — acceptable a11y trade-off, not a regression.** The 3 menus moved from a `document`-level Escape listener
    to a **container-level** one. Since the hook moves focus INTO the menu on open, Escape works under normal flow; if focus ever left the
    menu without closing it, the click-outside backdrop (z-20, present on all 3) still dismisses. Container-scoped Escape is the canonical
    focus-trap idiom. The 2 new Playwright tests assert the real path (focus-in → Escape-close → return-focus-to-trigger); selectors verified
    against DOM (`+ New` → `New Client` dialog; `Columns` → `Toggle columns` menu first checkbox).
  - **CpvPage — correctness IMPROVEMENT.** `role`/`aria-modal` were MOVED off the outer `fixed inset-0` backdrop onto the inner panel
    (CpvPage.tsx:37-38) — aria-modal belongs on the dialog, not the backdrop. Net a11y fix, in-scope.
  - **Scope discipline (Karpathy) — surgically clean.** 10 tracked files + 1 new hook + e2e; +151/-42. Replaced 3 bespoke document-Escape

- **2026-06-09 — B-8/B-9 Hexagon loader + loading time-bands (working tree, pre-commit; NEW
  `apps/web/src/components/ui/HexagonLoader.tsx` + NEW `apps/web/src/lib/useLoadingBand.ts` +
  `data-grid/DataGrid.tsx` + `index.css` + 1 e2e). Implements PAGINATION_AND_LOADING_STANDARDS §6/§7/§8/§9 on the
  Universal DataGrid → all 8 lists. VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit AFTER one pre-commit gate — both new files are
  UNTRACKED; the §6/§8 reconciliation is SOUND, not a frozen-standard violation, no ADR needed).** Re-audited the
  diff adversarially; ran web tsc + eslint myself; traced the band/tbody state machine and the test route-glob rather
  than rubber-stamp.
  - **🎯 THE KEY DESIGN DECISION (indeterminate-for-list-loads) — HONORS the frozen standard; NOT a §6 violation, no
    ADR required.** §6 row-3 (1–3 s) reads "loader + percentage", but **§8 is the governing, unconditional rule**
    ("Percentages MUST reflect actual work stages — never an animated guess"). §6's "+ percentage" presumes a
    *stageable* operation — its own §8 canonical maps are report/MIS/case-creation jobs, never a list fetch. A single
    list GET is genuinely one-stage (one round-trip, no observable intermediate progress), so a % there would BE the
    "animated guess" §8 forbids. Independently, **§9 governs *table loading* and mandates skeleton rows — not a
    percentage** — so a list is explicitly a skeleton/indeterminate surface, not a staged-% surface. The CTO correctly
    reserves determinate % for the §8 staged jobs (reports/MIS/exports — the operations phase) and uses indeterminate
    (a marching dash segment, no number) for list loads. This APPLIES §8 to resolve §6's general phrasing; it does not
    reopen the freeze. Both new-file doc comments state this rationale honestly (`HexagonLoader.tsx:9-11`,
    `useLoadingBand.ts:3-11`). **Ruling: in-spec.**
  - **B-9 (geometric loader) — SATISFIED, no forbidden style.** `HexagonLoader.tsx` is an SVG hexagon `<polygon>`
    outline (HEX_POINTS) + a second stroked polygon — no `<circle>` spin, no `<progress>`/bar, no bouncing dots.
    Determinate fills via `stroke-dashoffset` over `pathLength=100` (+ center `{value}%`, clamped 0–100,
    `Math.round`); indeterminate marches a `25 75` dash via `.hex-march` (index.css `@keyframes acs-hex-march`,
    1.2 s linear). `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` → `animation:none` static hexagon, `role=status`/`aria-live=polite`
    text still announces. Tokens-only (`stroke-border`/`stroke-primary`/`text-foreground`/`text-muted-foreground` — all
    real semantic tokens, tokens.css), zero hex/rgb in added lines.
  - **B-8 (skeleton now band-gated) — ADVANCED correctly.** Old `showSkeleton = isLoading` (skeleton from t=0 →
    flicker). New `useLoadingBand(isLoading)` → `none`(0–300 ms)/`skeleton`(300 ms–1 s)/`loader`(1–3 s)/`loader-op`(≥3 s),
    cleared on inactive. `showSkeleton = band==='skeleton'`; `showLoader = band==='loader'||'loader-op'`. State-machine
    traced over the 4 tbody branches (DataGrid.tsx:528/539/547/558/566): band=none → all 4 false → empty tbody (§6
    no-flicker ✓); skeleton → skeleton rows; loader → Hexagon (operation text only from loader-op, §6 ✓); loaded → data.
    Rollout is UNIVERSAL by construction — the change lives in the single shared `<DataGrid>` core; all 8 lists funnel
    through it (6 direct: cases/locations/rates/templates/users/VU + clients/products via MasterDataCrud). No per-page
    wiring, no list left behind.
  - **Regression scan — empty/error/no-flicker all SOUND, one one-frame cosmetic flicker.** error/empty/data branches
    were re-gated from `!showSkeleton` to `!isLoading` — this is an IMPROVEMENT: during first load `isLoading=T`
    suppresses the "No records" empty-state, so it can no longer flash before rows arrive (the naive bug). **SHOULD-FIX
    (non-blocking, cosmetic):** `showLoader` is gated on `band`, NOT on `isLoading`; on the resolve frame React Query
    flips `isLoading→false` but the hook's `setBand('none')` runs in a post-paint effect, so for ONE render
    `band==='loader'` AND `!isLoading` are both true → the Hexagon row and the real data rows co-render for a single
    frame (no crash, self-corrects next tick). Cheap fix: `const showLoader = isLoading && (band==='loader'||'loader-op')`.
    Flag, don't block.

    `getByRole('status',{name:/loading/i})` visible then hidden + grid renders. Route-glob disambiguation is SOUND:

    matches. 1.8 s lands in the loader band (>1 s, <3 s) → indeterminate, no operation text — matches the impl.

- **2026-06-09 — Row-select + bulk actions, sub-slice 1 (reference) — DATAGRID_STANDARD §15 selection on the shared
  DataGrid + built-in Export-Selected (B-13 mode 2), wired on clients/products ONLY (working tree, pre-commit; 11 files,
  +263/-18). VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit). NO new files → no `git add` trap this slice (confirmed `git status` = 0
  untracked).** Re-audited the diff adversarially; traced the export-mode ternary, the empty-ids guard, and the
  select-all-matching path myself rather than trust the summary.
  - **🎯 SCOPE / SEQUENCING — the CTO's self-flagged question, RULED: committing this reference sub-slice now is
    ACCEPTABLE, NOT a half-done rollout.** The selection infra lives in ONE place — the shared `DataGrid.tsx` core (the
    `selectable`/`bulkActions` props, `BulkSelection` type, checkbox column, bar, select-all-matching banner) — and is
    OPTED-IN by exactly one consumer this slice: `MasterDataCrud.tsx:133` (`selectable`), which backs clients+products
    only. The other 6 lists are inert (no `selectable` prop → no checkbox column, byte-identical render). This is the
    SAME contract-then-consumer cadence the panel has blessed all rollout long (sort→header-UI, filter-contract→grid-UI,
    DataGrid reference→per-list rollout): build the lever on the reference, prove it end-to-end, THEN roll. It is a
    coherent, independently-shippable, fully-working vertical slice (clients/products genuinely select + Export-Selected
    today, live-browser-proven), not a dangling stub. The Karpathy finish-one-thing rule bars *pivoting to a different
    registry item* mid-task — it does NOT bar landing a deliberately-scoped first slice of THIS item with the remaining
    sub-slices (2 = roll `selectable`+Export-Selected to VU/users/templates/locations/rates; 3 = page-specific bulk
    activate/deactivate via the `bulkActions` prop) explicitly tracked as the immediate next sub-slices. Ruling: in-scope,
    sequencing sound, NOT creep. (Carrying sub-slices 2+3 as OPEN below so they don't drift — the item stays "in
    progress" on the ledger until the rollout + bulk-mutations land.)
  - **🔍 The empty-ids "export nothing" guard (the load-bearing correctness check — a bug here = exporting the WHOLE
    table when nothing's ticked) — CORRECT, defence-in-depth, test-proven.** Service (`clients/service.ts:68-71`,
    `products/service.ts` mirror byte-identical): `selectedIds = mode==='selected' ? ex.ids.map(Number).filter(Number.isInteger)
    : undefined`; then `if (mode==='selected' && (!selectedIds || selectedIds.length===0)) return { rows:[], columns }`
    — a malformed/empty id set (`ids=abc`, or `mode=selected` with no `ids` at all) yields header-only, NEVER a
    fall-through to all. The repo (`repository.ts:42-46`) only appends `id = ANY($n)` when `o.ids?.length`, and the
    service guarantees a non-empty array when it passes `ids` (early-return otherwise) — so the two layers agree, no
    "ids present but empty array reaches SQL" path. Test-proven both ways: `clients.api.test.ts` — `mode=selected&ids=<a>`
    → only SELA, NOT SELB (excludes unticked); `mode=selected` no ids → `split('\r\n')` length 1 (header only). The guard
    is genuinely the inverse of the dangerous default.
  - **No regression to the existing `current`/`all` export modes — the ternary flip is behaviour-preserving (verified by
    truth-table).** `limit/offset` rewrote from `mode==='all' ? threshold : r.limit` to `mode==='current' ? r.limit :
    threshold` (and offset symmetric). Enumerated: `current`→r.limit/r.offset (unchanged); `all`→threshold/0 (unchanged);
    `selected`→threshold/0 (new, correct — the `id = ANY` filter bounds the set). `assertExportable` stays gated on
    `mode==='all'` ONLY — sound: `selected` is bounded by the ticked id list (and `current` by the page). `ex.ids` is
    ALWAYS present (`resolveExport` returns `ids:[]` for every mode — platform test updated to assert the `ids:[]` default
    + the `mode=selected ids=1,2,3` parse + `mode=bogus`→throw replacing the now-valid `selected`), so `ex.ids.map` never
    NPEs on a non-selected mode. The SDK `exportQueryToParams` drops the page window for BOTH `all` and `selected` and only
    emits `ids` for `selected` with a non-empty list — coherent with the server.
  - **"Select all N matching" → `mode='all'`, NOT a client-side id dump — CORRECT and the only scale-safe choice.** The
    banner sets `allMatching=true`; `exportSelection` then routes to `runExport(format,'all')` (DataGrid.tsx) which re-runs
    the query WITH the active `search`/`filters`/`sort` and IS 413-guarded by `assertExportable`. So select-all-matching
    exports the *filtered* set (not the whole table) and never holds every id client-side (`BulkSelection` doc + the
    inline comment both state this). Ticking/un-ticking any row resets `allMatching=false` (`toggleRow`/`togglePage`),
    correctly downgrading to explicit-id mode. The clear-on-`[search,sortBy,sortOrder,filtersKey]` effect (page NOT in
    deps) matches the stated "ephemeral; clears on search/sort/filter; accumulates across pages" §15 contract exactly.
  - **Frozen standards — clean.** Tokens-only on the bar + checkbox cells (`border-border`/`bg-surface-muted`/`text-foreground`/
    `text-primary`/`btn-ghost` — all real semantic tokens; zero hex/rgb/arbitrary-color in added lines). Responsive `.rtable`
    card model preserved — the new leading checkbox `<td>` carries `data-label=""` in the data row AND the skeleton row, and
    `colCount = visibleColumns.length + (selectable?1:0)` correctly widens the loader/error/empty `colSpan` so none under-spans
    the new column. a11y wired: `role=region aria-label="Bulk actions"`, `aria-live=polite` on the count, per-row
    `aria-label="Select row"`, header `aria-label="Select all rows on this page"` + `indeterminate` ref for the partial-page
    state, row checkbox `onClick` `stopPropagation` so ticking doesn't fire `onRowClick` nav. No `any`/suppression/`console.*`
    in added source (grep `^+` non-test = NONE). Append-only audit untouched; the export already logs an `event:'export'` line
    (mode now carries `selected`). RBAC untouched — the export route's existing `authorize` is unchanged (selection is a
    client-side narrowing of an already-authorized list; `id = ANY` is ANDed ON TOP of the server-side scope clause, so a
    hand-crafted out-of-scope id can't leak — the SDK doc comment states exactly this and it's true at the SQL level).
  - **Array→envelope #1-watch — N/A.** Export returns a file blob, not the list envelope; `ExportMode`/`ExportRequest`
    gained `'selected'`/`ids?` ADDITIVELY (ADR-0011 — no field removed, no consumer breaks; mobile reads neither). The only
    list-shape touch is the additive `ids?: number[]` on `ClientListOptions`/`ProductListOptions` (internal repo interface,
    not a wire contract). No bare-array regression.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, ×1) / NOTE:** `mode='selected'` is deliberately NOT `assertExportable`-guarded and sets
    `limit=exportThreshold()`; a hand-crafted `ids` list longer than the threshold would silently cap at the threshold count
    rather than 413. In practice selected ids come from user ticks accumulated across pages (bounded by what's reasonable to
    tick) and the `id = ANY` filter caps rows, so this is a tolerable, low-severity edge — flag, don't block. Optional: cap
    `ids.length` or 413 on selected too in a later touch.
  - **Gate accepted on recorded CTO evidence** (`pnpm verify` green; Playwright 12/12 datagrid incl. the new bulk-bar test
    [tick row → bar "1 selected" → Export XLSX visible → Clear hides bar]; live-browser: ticked a row → bar → Export XLSX →
    `GET /clients/export?…&mode=selected&ids=3` → 200) — independently traced the export-mode truth-table, the empty-ids
    guard both directions, the select-all-matching `all`-route, and confirmed clients/products are the ONLY opt-in
    (`selectable` appears once, in MasterDataCrud which also passes `exportFn`). **VERDICT: PASS — the §15 selection states
    are correct (bar, indeterminate header, select-all-matching banner→`all`), the empty-ids guard is the safe inverse of
    the dangerous default (test-proven), the `current`/`all` modes are behaviour-preserved, scope is surgical, and the
    reference-then-rollout sequencing is the panel's standard, blessed cadence — NOT a half-done rollout. Cleared to commit.**
  - **OPEN (carried forward — the row-select/bulk-actions item stays IN PROGRESS until these land):**
    - **Sub-slice 2** — roll `selectable` + Export-Selected to the remaining 5 admin lists (VU · users · templates ·
      locations · rates). Each needs its repo `ids?` filter + service `selected` guard mirrored (the clients/products

- **2026-06-09 — Row-select + bulk actions, sub-slice 3a — bulk activate/deactivate (reference = clients/products),
  per CONCURRENCY_AND_EDITING_STANDARD §1/§7 + DATAGRID_STANDARD §15 (working tree, pre-commit; 11 modified +263/-22,
  +3 NEW UNTRACKED files: `platform/bulk.ts`, `components/BulkStatusActions.tsx`, `packages/sdk/src/bulk.ts`).
  VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit — CONDITIONAL on `git add`-ing the 3 new files; see the hard gate).** Re-audited the
  diff adversarially; traced the OCC classification against `repo.setActive`, the `Set→Map` key-identity, the
  parse-before-apply ordering, and the partial-result UX myself rather than trust the summary.
  - **🎯 RULING #1 — the `allMatching`-disables-mutation decision is SOUND, in fact the only correct call.** You cannot
    do per-row OCC on rows whose `version` you don't hold. `allMatching` ("select all N matching") deliberately never
    loads the off-page row objects (the scale-safe design blessed in sub-slice 1 — never dump every id/row client-side),
    so `selection.rows` is empty and there's no version to guard on. `BulkStatusActions.tsx:57-60` correctly REFUSES the
    versioned mutation in that mode and shows "Tick individual rows to activate / deactivate." — export still works at
    scale (it routes to the server-side `all` query, no client-side ids). This is the honest boundary: a versioned bulk
    write requires the user to materialize the rows (tick them, capturing versions), exactly as the sub-slice-1 OPEN item
    predicted ("the `allMatching` path will need a server-side act-on-all endpoint since ids aren't held client-side —
    design that contract when it lands, don't dump ids"). That server-side act-on-all-matching endpoint is NOT built here
    and correctly so — it's a separate, larger contract (it would need its own OCC story: act under the active filter,
    not under captured versions). Disabling rather than faking it is the disciplined choice. NOT a gap — a stated boundary.
  - **🎯 RULING #2 — the partial-success UX is HONEST: conflicts are surfaced, never swallowed.** `applyBulkOcc`
    (`platform/bulk.ts:60-86`) classifies each row against the resource's EXISTING OCC write (`repo.setActive`): a stale
    row throws `AppError.stale` → code `STALE_UPDATE` → CONFLICT; a missing row throws `AppError.notFound` → status 404 →
    NOT_FOUND; **anything else rethrows** (a real failure is never laundered into a per-row status). Verified against
    `repository.ts:171/177` (notFound on absent row, `AppError.stale(before)` on version-mismatch UPDATE returning 0 rows)
    and `errors.ts:35/55` (notFound→404, stale→409/`STALE_UPDATE`) — the classification is exact. The FE
    (`BulkStatusActions.tsx:43-49`) renders "N updated · M changed by someone else · K not found" and — the load-bearing
    bit — **clears the selection ONLY on a clean run** (`!conflictCount && !notFoundCount`), keeping it on partial so the
    message + the conflicting rows stay on screen. No silent overwrite anywhere: a row changed since it was ticked comes
    back CONFLICT and is left untouched (test-proven, see below). This satisfies §1's "no silent overwrite, ever" and §7's
    "mixed batch → per-row result (success/CONFLICT), no partial silent overwrite; … else per-row" — per-row (non-atomic)
    is EXPLICITLY permitted by the standard (line 93-94); atomic-transaction is the "where the batch must be atomic"
    alternative, not a requirement for (de)activate. The 500-cap (`MAX_BULK_ITEMS=500`) matches "large bulk = background
    job" (§7 line 119). Mid-batch infra failure → 500 with rows-so-far committed (each `setActive` is its own txn): within
    the per-row spec and NOT silent (caller gets 500, not a false OK). Sound.
  - **`Set<string>` → `Map<string,T>` refactor — key-identity preserved, no off-by-one selection bug.** The Map is keyed
    by `String(rowId(row))`; the checkbox checks `selectedRows.has(row.id)` where TanStack `row.id` is
    `getRowId:(row)=>String(rowId(row))` (`DataGrid.tsx:304`) → the stored key and the lookup key are byte-identical, so
    tick/untick/has all agree (same invariant the prior `Set` relied on). `togglePage` now stores row OBJECTS
    (`items.forEach((r)=>next.set(String(rowId(r)), r))`, DataGrid.tsx:352) not just ids — correct, the version must be
    captured. `bulkSelection.ids = [...keys]`, `.rows = [...values]` stay consistent; `exportSelection` reads
    `[...selectedRows.keys()]` so Export-Selected (sub-slice 1) is byte-behaviour-preserved. `BulkSelection<T>` going
    generic is additive (re-exported from the data-grid barrel; `bulkActions?:(sel:BulkSelection<T>)=>ReactNode`).
  - **parse-before-apply = "drops nothing silently → 400" HOLDS.** `parseBulkItems` (`bulk.ts:36-53`) fully validates the
    WHOLE batch (array non-empty, ≤500, each `{id,version}` well-typed, id matches the resource's `idKind` int|uuid via a
    UUID regex) and THROWS on the first malformed item BEFORE `applyBulkOcc` runs any write — so a bad item #3 means items
    #1-2 are never written (no partial-but-wrong batch). Over-cap → 400 with zero writes. `idKind:'int'` here keeps a
    non-int id out of SQL (defence-in-depth atop the parameterized `setActive`).
  - **Scope discipline (Karpathy) — surgical, traces 1:1 to "bulk (de)activate on the reference."** 3 new platform/SDK/FE
    primitives + clients/products ×{service(+bulkSetActive),controller(+bulkActivate/bulkDeactivate),routes(+2 POSTs)} +
    the DataGrid Set→Map + MasterDataCrud wiring (`bulkActions` prop) + the data-grid barrel + sdk index + clients api
    tests. NO new write path invented — `bulkSetActive` REUSES the version-guarded `repo.setActive` per row (bulk.ts
    docstring + service.ts make this explicit). No schema/migration (none needed — `version` already on these tables,
    `setActive` already OCC-guarded + append-only-audited; the bulk layer is pure orchestration). Products mirrors clients
    byte-identical (verified). No adjacent "improvement," no speculative abstraction.
  - **Route ordering — collision-safe + commented.** `/bulk-activate|/bulk-deactivate` are static single-segment POSTs
    declared BEFORE `/:id/activate` (two-segment) in both routers, with an inline comment stating the no-collision
    reasoning. Express won't capture `bulk-activate` as `:id` because the bulk paths have no second segment and are matched
    first. Both routes reuse the EXACT sibling perm `MASTERDATA_MANAGE` — no new authz surface; test-proven (FA→403,
    unauth→401). RBAC default-deny intact.
  - **Frozen standards — clean.** Tokens-only on the bulk bar (`text-muted-foreground`, `btn-ghost`, `role="status"` —
    real classes/semantic tokens; zero hex/rgb/arbitrary-color in added lines or the 3 new files, grepped). No
    `any`/suppression/`@ts-`/`console.*` in any added line or new file (grepped both). Append-only audit untouched —

    perm 403/401.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, ×1 — the one real nuance):** on a PARTIAL result the selection is kept (good — message +
    rows stay), but the kept `selectedRows` Map still holds the STALE row objects (old versions). `qc.invalidateQueries`
    refetches the LIST grid, but the selection Map is not re-synced from the fresh rows, so an immediate Activate/Deactivate
    RE-CLICK re-sends the same stale versions → the conflicting rows perpetually CONFLICT until the user manually re-ticks
    them (which re-captures fresh versions). The code comment (BulkStatusActions.tsx:47-48) correctly says "re-tick the
    conflicting rows and retry" — re-tick IS the working escape and it's documented, so the UX is HONEST, not misleading.
    Optional polish next touch: after a partial run, drop the OK'd rows from the selection (keep only conflicts) and/or
    re-sync kept rows' versions from the refetched page so a bare retry can succeed. Flag, don't block.
  - **VERDICT: PASS — per-row OCC with a per-row result and zero silent overwrite (test-proven), the partial-failure UX is
    honest (conflicts surfaced + selection kept), the `allMatching`-disables-mutation decision is the only correct call
    (no versions held → no OCC possible; export still scales), scope is surgical (reuses `setActive`, invents no second
    write path), route ordering + RBAC + tokens + append-only audit all clean. Cleared to commit ONCE the 3 new files are

- **2026-06-10 — Locations multi-area create (v1-parity gap) — full-stack (sdk `locations.ts`+`client.ts`+contract/transport tests; api `locations/{service,controller,routes}`+5 api-tests; web `LocationsPage.tsx` area-chips). VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit).** Audited the working-tree diff adversarially against the frozen standards + traced the load-bearing facts (LOCATION_EXISTS throw site, route order, ZodError→400, central error map) at the source rather than trust the summary.
  - **No FROZEN reopen — flat catalog model intact.** The change adds ONLY a fan-out wrapper: one shared pincode/city/state/country + N areas → N independent `(pincode,area)` rows via the existing audited single `create`. No new table, no migration (`db/v2/migrations` not in diff), no column/constraint/contract change to `Location` (the row shape is byte-identical; `LocationBatchResult` is a NEW additive response type for the NEW endpoint only). The flat pincode-centric model and ADR-0020 key-correctability are untouched. The shared-pincode design is the right one — it structurally prevents the same pincode drifting to a different city/state across its areas (the v1 footgun), enforced by the schema taking pincode/city/state ONCE.
  - **Route ordering + RBAC — correct.** `POST /batch` is a static single-segment path declared BEFORE `/:id` (routes.ts:28, with the rationale comment matching the file's established `/export`,`/import`,`/bulk-*` precedent) → never captured as id="batch". Verified no collision with the two-segment `/:id/activate`. Perm = `MASTERDATA_MANAGE`, identical to `POST /` create authority — exactly right (batch IS create); test proves FIELD_AGENT→403, unauth→401.
  - **Reuse over reinvention — exemplary, and the audit-per-row invariant HOLDS.** `createBatch` calls `locationService.create({...shared, area}, userId)` in a loop; each call runs the audited repo `create` which appends its own `audit_log` CREATE inside the row txn (repository.ts:132-142). NO new raw insert path was introduced. This mirrors the already-blessed `importConfirm` pattern (service.ts:163-171, which also fans out to the same `create` for per-row audit) — consistent with house precedent.
  - **Bug/risk lens — clean.** (a) **Partial-failure semantics correct:** the `catch` narrows to `e instanceof AppError && e.code==='LOCATION_EXISTS'` → push to `skipped`+continue; ANYTHING ELSE rethrows (`throw e`) → propagates to `next(e)` → central handler. Verified `LOCATION_EXISTS` is the EXACT code the repo throws on the unique `(pincode,area)` violation via `isUniqueViolation` (repository.ts:146-150); a genuine DB/internal error is NOT swallowed. (b) **N txns for N areas** — each `create` is its own transaction (no outer wrapping txn), so a mid-batch skip/failure leaves prior rows committed; this is the INTENDED "never aborts the rest" semantics, not a leak — and it's honest because the response enumerates exactly what was `created` vs `skipped`. (c) **In-request dedupe** is case-insensitive (`toLowerCase` Set), case-preserving in output, ordered-first-wins. (d) **FE triple-path converges:** Enter/comma `addAreas`, `onBlur` flush, and the mutationFn folding still-uncommitted `areaInput` all run through the SAME case-insensitive de-dupe before POST, so the "text left in the box" path can't double-submit or drop an area; the disabled-button gate `!(areas.length || areaInput.trim())` correctly still allows submit when the user typed one area and never pressed Enter. Chip remove (`filter x!==a`) + `key={a}` are safe because case-collisions can't coexist as chips.
  - **Tests adequate — all five required cases present + green.** created-N (201, shared pincode/city asserted, totalCount=3), in-request case-insensitive dedupe→`skipped:'duplicate in request'`, pre-existing `(pincode,area)`→`skipped:'pincode+area already exists'` without aborting the rest (totalCount=2), empty `areas`→400 VALIDATION (schema `.min(1)`), RBAC 403/401. Scope is surgical: every changed file traces to the multi-area slice; the one-line page-subtitle copy tweak is incidental-but-harmless.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, ×1):** the FE `notice` ("Added N areas; skipped M already-existing") collapses BOTH skip reasons into "already-existing" — an in-request duplicate is reported to the user as "already-existing" even though the server distinguishes `duplicate in request` vs `pincode+area already exists`. Cosmetic (the FE already de-dupes in-request before POST, so server-side `duplicate in request` is near-unreachable from the UI); tidy the copy on next touch if desired. Not a defect.

- **2026-06-10 — User-Management parity Slice 3: extend `users` with v1 profile fields (migration 0025 + SDK contracts + repo/service + FE form rebuild). VERDICT: PASS — cleared to commit. No BLOCK; one FLAG-as-UX-note (non-blocking), no SHOULD-FIX.**
  - **(1) Design split — SOUND.** Nullable-DB / optional-CreateUserSchema / required-FE is the correct shape: it keeps the FK-free import, the seed admin (0009), and the auth/cases/rates fixtures alive (they create users with no phone/dept/designation) while the interactive form enforces the v1 parity. `employee_id` is the one always-present field (server-minted from `user_employee_seq`, UNIQUE) — never client-supplied.   - **(2) Migration 0025 — forward-only + idempotent + triple-written.** `CREATE SEQUENCE IF NOT EXISTS` + 5× `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` + 2× `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` + backfill `WHERE employee_id IS NULL` + UNIQUE via **`pg_constraint`-name guard** (correct: a UNIQUE constraint owns a backing index of the same name → a re-run raises 42P07 `duplicate_table`, NOT `duplicate_object`, so the existence guard is the right idiom — catching the SQLSTATE would be brittle). FK cols nullable; `password_must_change` is the lone NOT-NULL (DEFAULT false — safe). Ordering correct (0023 departments → 0024 designations → 0025 FKs) → replayable on a fresh DB. **Verified LIVE in BOTH containers** (dev `crm2_dev_pg`/db `crm2_dev` :54329 + test `crm2_test_pg`/db `crm2_test` :5433): all 5 cols present (4 nullable, `password_must_change` NOT NULL), seq=1, uq=1, idx_dept=1, FK→departments=1, **null_emp=0** (backfill ran). File + 2 live DBs = triple-write confirmed.
  - **(3) Password-param cast bug — FIXED & holds.** CREATE INSERT writes `$10::text` in BOTH spots (`password_hash = $10::text` AND `CASE WHEN $10::text IS NOT NULL THEN now() ELSE NULL END`) — the cast is required because a bare null bind in a CASE has no inferable type → "could not determine data type of parameter $10" → 500 on EVERY create. Both casts present. **Param numbering verified line-by-line**: INSERT $1..$11 ↔ values `[username,name,email,phone,departmentId,designationId,role,reportsTo,effectiveFrom??null,passwordHash??null,userId]` (userId bound once, reused as created_by+updated_by via `$11,$11`).   - **(4) COUNT-join safety — CLEAN.** COUNT stays `FROM users u` (join-free); the dept/design LEFT JOINs are on the ITEMS query only. `sortMap` has only `reportsTo:'m.name'` (pre-existing) + real `u.*` cols — `departmentName`/`designationName` are NOT sortable. `filterMap` is `FROM users u`-only (username/name/role/createdAt/effectiveFrom) — the joined names are NOT filterable → no COUNT-vs-items clause divergence, no fan-out (1:1 LEFT JOINs on PK).
  - **(5) Security — PASS.** Optional initial password gated by `StrongPasswordSchema` (≥8 + lower+upper+digit+symbol, max 200) in zod BEFORE hashing; hashed via platform `hashPassword` (scrypt, ADR-0014, salted) in the service; written only to `password_hash`/`password_set_at` (WRITE-only). `COLS` (read) + `User`/`UserView` SDK interfaces carry NO password field → never returned. `employee_id` minted server-side, never accepted from client. RBAC unchanged (USER_VIEW read / USER_MANAGE write). FK violation 23503 → 400 INVALID_REFERENCE (test-covered: dept 999999).
  - **(6) Conventions — clean.** snake-SQL / camel-TS; grep over all changed non-SQL files = ZERO `console.*`, `eslint-disable`, `: any`, hex colors. `tsc --noEmit` clean across web+api+sdk; `eslint` clean on the 4 changed TS files.
