- **2026-06-10 — User-Management parity Slice 4: password & login security (strong-password policy on set+change, self-service `/auth/change-password`, admin generate-one-time-password + unlock, 5-strike account lockout w/ 15-min auto-unlock; migration `0026_auth_lockout.sql`). VERDICT: PASS — cleared to commit. One LOW-sev accepted-tradeoff FLAG, no BLOCK.** Re-audited the full diff adversarially + ran every gate myself rather than rubber-stamp.
  - **(1) Security — lockout sound.** `recordFailedLogin` is a SINGLE atomic `UPDATE … SET failed_login_count = failed_login_count + 1, locked_until = CASE WHEN failed_login_count + 1 >= $2 THEN now()+($3||' seconds')::interval ELSE locked_until END … RETURNING` — the increment + lock decision happen in one statement under the row lock, so concurrent failed logins can't lost-update (it's `count+1` in-SQL, not app read-modify-write). Locks EXACTLY on the 5th failure (pre-increment 4 → `4+1>=5`); test-proven. `ELSE locked_until` means a 6th failure does NOT slide the window forward — fine/better. **`isLocked(creds.lockedUntil)` is checked BEFORE `verifyPassword` (service.ts:57)** so a locked account can't be probed; auto-unlock is implicit (`locked_until > now()` comparison, no write needed). Success → `resetLoginState` zeroes the counter + clears the lock. **Strong policy applied to BOTH `SetPasswordSchema` and `ChangePasswordSchema.newPassword` (both → `StrongPasswordSchema`) AND the minted one-time password** (`generateTempPassword`: one char drawn per class then Fisher–Yates shuffled with crypto `randomBytes` so no class is always in front — test asserts all 4 classes present; length 14; ambiguous chars excluded). `change-password` proves current → sets strong new → `revokeAllForUser` (forces re-auth on every other session). Passwords never logged/returned anywhere except the one-time plaintext, returned ONCE by design (`{temporaryPassword}`), shown once in the FE modal. No `console.*` of any secret (grep clean).
  - **(2) Mobile/contract (ADR-0012) — additive, no break.** `LoginResponse.mustChangePassword` is a new field mobile ignores (unknown-field tolerant). New **423 ACCOUNT_LOCKED** only on the lockout path (login was 401-only) — an additive failure mode an existing consumer already had to handle as "login failed"; the body still carries a generic `error` code. `change-password`/`generate-temp-password`/`unlock` are NEW routes. Zero existing shape/status changed for the happy path.
  - **(3) API-contract — correct.** Route ordering: `/:id/generate-temp-password` + `/:id/unlock` are two-segment under `/:id` (mirrors `/:id/activate`, no collision with the single-segment bulk routes); `/auth/change-password` is a new static route on the auth router. RBAC: generate-temp/unlock gated `USER_MANAGE` (admin-tier); `change-password` is authenticated-any-user via `requireUserId(req)` (401 when `req.auth` absent — `authenticate()` is global+non-rejecting, the controller helper is the gate, test-proven 401). SDK methods additive; `client.test` count **81→84** (`toBe(84)`) holds.
  - **(4) DB — migration 0026 forward-only + idempotent** (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` ×2); `failed_login_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`, `locked_until timestamptz` nullable. **Triple-write VERIFIED LIVE** (I queried both containers): dev `crm2_dev`@:54329 AND test `crm2_test`@:5433 both show the two new cols with the exact types/nullability/default. `password_must_change` correctly reused from 0025 (not re-added).
  - **(5) Bugs — none found.** No off-by-one (locks on 5th, verified). No race (atomic SQL). The lint `no-warning-comments` ban on the term `temp` is RESPECTED — grep for a standalone `temp` token in comments of all changed files = ZERO (function identifier `generateTempPassword` is not a comment; `eslint .` exits clean). 423 added to `HTTP_STATUS.LOCKED`.
  - **(6) Conventions — clean.** Named constants `MAX_FAILED_LOGINS=5` / `LOCKOUT_COOLDOWN_S=900` (no magic numbers); snake-SQL/camel-TS; no `console.*`/`eslint-disable`/`: any` in added lines (grep clean). Scope surgical — every changed line traces to the slice. `parseId` UUID-validates the user id (IDOR-safe 400 on miss); `userId(req)` threaded as `updated_by` for the audit trail on temp-password + unlock writes.
  - **Gates GREEN (ran them, DATABASE_URL=…:5433/crm2_test):** **API 404/404** across 17 files (auth file = 15, incl. the +6 slice-4: lockout-then-admin-unlock, success-resets-counter, temp-pw→login `mustChangePassword=true`→change clears it, change-pw wrong-current 401 + weak-new 400, no-auth 401, normal-login `mustChangePassword=false`). **SDK 77/77** (`client.test` 84-call assertion intact). `eslint .` clean. `pnpm verify` typecheck/lint/format/boundaries/build all pass (the lone red is the documented false-RED: a bare `verify` with no `DATABASE_URL` skips integration tests and `assertExportable`'s `loadEnv` 500s on the missing env — NOT this slice; the full suite is 404/404 with the DB wired).
  - **FLAG (LOW-sev, accepted trade-off — record, not block):** the lockout introduces a username-enumeration oracle — a LOCKED known user returns **423** while an unknown user returns **401**. An attacker who burns 5 attempts on a guessed username learns it exists (423 vs 401). This is inherent to a user-facing lockout (the 423 exists precisely to tell a legitimate user WHY they're refused) and is v1/industry-standard parity; mitigations (generic 401 + silent lockout, or IP-based throttling) are a deliberate product trade-off, not a defect. ACCEPTED. NOTE: lockout is per-account only — no IP/global rate-limit, so an attacker can still spray DIFFERENT usernames; pair with edge/WAF rate-limiting at GA (carry).
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit.** OBSERVATION (carried, FE-wide, unchanged): admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered (server-side 403 is the boundary).

- **2026-06-10 — User-Management parity Slice 5: MFA / TOTP (RFC 6238 over node:crypto, AES-256-GCM secret-at-rest, 10 one-time recovery codes, login challenge + admin force/disable; migration 0027). VERDICT: PASS — 1 LOW-sev hardening FLAG + 1 dead-code SHOULD-FIX, no BLOCK.** Re-audited the full diff adversarially + ran the static gates myself (DBs not bootable in this sandbox → live triple-write + DB-bound flow tests deferred to the implementer, see gates note).
  - **(1) TOTP correctness — CORRECT.** HOTP (RFC 4226) dynamic truncation is textbook: `offset = hmac[19] & 0xf`, big-endian 4-byte assembly with `& 0x7f` on the top byte then `& 0xff` on the rest, `bin % 10**6` zero-padded to 6. Counter is a true 8-byte big-endian write (`writeUInt32BE(high32,0)` + `writeUInt32BE(counter>>>0,4)`) — not the common 32-bit-only bug. base32 encode/decode are RFC 4648 (5-bit accumulator, A–Z2–7, no padding); the test pins the canonical vector `base32('foobar')='MZXW6YTBOI'` and a generate→totp→verify round-trip. `verifyTotp` rejects non-6-digit up front (`/^\d{6}$/` after whitespace strip), scans the ±1 step (`DRIFT_WINDOW=1`, 30s) window, and compares with `timingSafeEqual` GUARDED by an equal-length check (timingSafeEqual throws on length mismatch — the guard is mandatory and present). All constants named (`STEP_SECONDS/DIGITS/SECRET_BYTES/DRIFT_WINDOW/B32_BITS/...`), no magic numbers. Secret is 160-bit (`SECRET_BYTES=20`, RFC-recommended) from `randomBytes`.
  - **(2) Secret-at-rest — SOUND.** AES-256-GCM, fresh 12-byte random IV per `encryptSecret` (test asserts two encrypts of the same secret differ), auth tag captured + `setAuthTag` enforced on decrypt (tampered-ct test throws). Key = `scryptSync(MFA_ENC_KEY, fixed-salt, 32)` cached — fixed salt is acceptable here because the env key IS the secret and scrypt is only stretching it (documented in-file). Stored format `v1:iv:tag:ct` (base64) is version-tagged + length-validated on decrypt. The decrypted secret is NEVER returned after enrol-start (enroll/start returns only the base32 `secret` for manual setup + the otpauth URI; the encrypted blob is decrypted only transiently inside verify/login, never logged — grep clean). Dev-default key `dev-only-insecure-mfa-key-change-me` is clearly marked dev-only with an in-schema comment "set a real value in prod" (mirrors `JWT_SECRET`'s dev default) — **prod MUST override (carry as a deploy-gate note; same posture already accepted for JWT_SECRET).**
  - **(3) Recovery codes — CORRECT.** 10 codes (`RECOVERY_CODE_COUNT`), each base32 of 8 random bytes sliced to 10 chars, dash-grouped `XXXXX-XXXXX`; stored ONLY as scrypt hashes (`hashPassword(normRecovery(c))`), returned plaintext exactly ONCE from enroll/verify. Single-use: verify scans UNUSED hashes (`recoveryCodeUsed[i]` skip), `verifyPassword` (constant-time) matches, then `markRecoveryUsed` flips the parallel bool array (1-based pg index `i+1`). **Normalisation is consistent on BOTH mint and verify** (`normRecovery` = uppercase + strip non-alphanumeric) so dash/case formatting can't cause a false-miss. Test proves burn (reuse → MFA_REQUIRED).
  - **(4) Login challenge — CORRECT + ordering-safe.** `mfaEnrolled` = `m.user_id IS NOT NULL AND m.enrolled_at IS NOT NULL` (a PENDING row with `enrolled_at NULL` does NOT gate login → a half-finished enrolment can't lock the user out; the "must_enrol" test proves an mfa_required-but-unenrolled user still logs in with `mustEnrollMfa=true`). **MFA is verified strictly AFTER `verifyPassword` (service.ts:101→107)** — an attacker without the password reaches `invalidCreds()` and never probes MFA. Missing/invalid code → 401 MFA_REQUIRED (same status as a bad password); the code-vs-password distinction it leaks is exactly what an authenticated-FE needs (reveal the code field) and is the standard challenge UX — acceptable.
  - **(5) Mobile/contract (ADR-0012) — additive, no break.** `LoginSchema.mfaCode` optional + `LoginResponse.mustEnrollMfa` additive (unknown-field-tolerant mobile ignores both); `MFA_REQUIRED` is a NEW 401 code on the EXISTING login route — an enrolled user on an MFA-ignorant client simply sees a failed login (no crash; mobile users won't have enrolled via the web-only SecurityPage). 5 new auth routes additive. No `/api/v2` bump.
  - **(6) RBAC / route safety — CORRECT.** enroll/status/disable derive the subject from `requireUserId(req)` = `req.auth.userId` (NEVER a param) → a user can only act on SELF; `authenticate()` is global+non-rejecting so the controller helper is the 401 gate (test: unauth status/start → 401). admin-disable is `authorize(USER_MANAGE)` + `:userId` param (admin authority — intended cross-user, not IDOR; UUID not validated at the route but `deleteMfa` is an idempotent DELETE-by-PK → a bad id is a harmless no-op, no error leak). `mfa_required` is settable ONLY through `UpdateUserSchema` (USER_MANAGE).
  - **(7) DB — migration 0027 forward-only + idempotent** (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS users.mfa_required` + `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS user_mfa_secrets`); FK `user_id → users ON DELETE CASCADE` (a deleted user's secret is reaped); parallel `recovery_code_hashes`/`recovery_code_used` arrays kept consistent (`confirmEnrolment` rebuilds `used` as `array_agg(false)` over the hashes via `unnest`, so they're always equal length; mint always produces exactly 10). **Triple-write (file+dev:54329+test:5433) NOT verifiable in this sandbox (DBs not running) — implementer must confirm before commit.**
  - **(8) Conventions — clean.** No magic numbers (all named consts); no new dependency (node:crypto only, per policy); grep over the changed non-SQL files = ZERO `console.*`/`eslint-disable`/`: any`; the `no-warning-comments` `temp` ban is respected (the only match is "attempt" in a pre-existing comment). `tsc --noEmit` clean on api+web; `eslint` clean on every changed/new TS/TSX file.
  - **Gates (what I could run here): API TOTP+encryption unit suite 6/6 PASS** (`DATABASE_URL=… vitest run src/platform/__tests__/totp.test.ts` — the 2 encryption tests only fail with NO env because `loadEnv()` validates the whole schema; pass once any DATABASE_URL is set). **SDK 77/77** (full client.test green — note the prompt's "84→89" is stale; the repo gate is `sdk 77` and that holds). **API tsc 0 / web tsc 0 / eslint 0.** **DEFERRED to implementer (DB-bound, sandbox has no PG): the +6 MFA flow tests (enrol→MFA_REQUIRED→code-login→recovery-burn→admin-disable→mustEnrollMfa) and the live triple-write check** — the test code is present and well-shaped (reviewed line-by-line) but needs `DATABASE_URL` + migrated DBs to execute; run `pnpm verify` with the DB wired before commit.
  - **FLAG (LOW-sev, hardening — record, not block):** an invalid `mfaCode` on login does NOT increment the account-lockout counter (only a wrong PASSWORD does). An attacker who already holds the valid password could brute-force TOTP codes unthrottled. Practically negligible (10^6 space, 3 valid codes per 30s window → ~3e-6/guess, and the password is already compromised in this threat model), and TOTP brute-force resistance is normally an edge/IP-rate-limit concern — but worth a counter or per-account MFA-attempt throttle at GA. Pairs with the Slice-4 "no IP/global rate-limit" carry.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, dead code):** `platform/jwt.ts` adds `signMfaToken`/`verifyMfaToken` (a challenge-token-exchange model) that NOTHING imports — the shipped design uses the same-request `mfaCode` model instead, and the helper's doc-comment references a `/auth/mfa/verify` route that does not exist. Remove both functions (and the misleading comment) before commit to avoid a confusing unused API surface, or wire them if a token-exchange flow was intended. Confirmed via grep: zero callers outside jwt.ts.
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit AFTER (i) the implementer runs the DB-bound API flow tests + live triple-write green, and (ii) the dead `sign/verifyMfaToken` is removed (or the misleading comment fixed).** OBSERVATION (carried, FE-wide, unchanged): admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered (server-side 403 is the boundary).

- **2026-06-10 — User-Management parity Slice 6: SESSIONS (active-session view/revoke for self + admin, built on existing `auth_refresh_tokens`; migration `0028_session_tracking.sql` adds `ip inet` + `last_used_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now()`). Panel: CEO/Quality + Security + API-Contract + DB. PER-LENS: Security PASS · API-Contract PASS · DB PASS · Quality PASS. OVERALL VERDICT: PASS — cleared to commit. 2 LOW-sev FLAGs (one carried), no BLOCK, no must-fix.** Re-audited the full `git diff` adversarially, read the migration + 0009 base DDL + app wiring, and ran the gates myself (incl. live triple-write) rather than rubber-stamp.
  - **(1) Security / IDOR — SOUND (the load-bearing property).** Self routes derive the subject from `requireUserId(req)` = `req.auth.userId`, **NEVER a path param** (controller.ts listSessions/revokeSession) — a user can only see/revoke their OWN sessions. Revoke is owner-scoped IN SQL: `revokeRefreshForUser(jti,userId)` = `UPDATE … WHERE jti=$1 AND user_id=$2 AND revoked_at IS NULL RETURNING jti` → returns false when the jti isn't an ACTIVE session of THIS user (unknown / already-revoked / **belongs to someone else**), which the service maps to **404 SESSION_NOT_FOUND**. So a cross-user revoke and a non-existent jti are INDISTINGUISHABLE (both 404) — no enumeration oracle, no info leak, IDOR-safe. **Test-proven LIVE:** Alice POSTing Bob's real jti → 404 + Bob's session untouched; double-revoke → 404. `currentJti` query param is NOT an injection/IDOR vector — it's bound as `$2` in `COALESCE(jti=$2,false)` (a read-only boolean flag on the caller's OWN list), never interpolated, and reveals nothing the caller doesn't already own (it only labels which of *their* rows is "this device"). No refresh-token SECRET is ever exposed: `sessionsForUser` SELECTs only `jti AS id, device_id, device_info, ip::text, last_used_at, created_at, current` — the jti is a denylist HANDLE (revoking it can't mint a token), not the signed refresh JWT. Admin routes correctly gated `authorize(USER_MANAGE)` (test: a MANAGER → 403; SUPER_ADMIN → 200); admin cross-user list/revoke is intended authority, not IDOR. Self routes 401 when unauthenticated (test-proven).
  - **(2) API-contract — CORRECT.** Route ordering under `/users/:id/*` is collision-free: `GET /:id/sessions` (2-seg) and `POST /:id/sessions/:jti/revoke` (3-seg) are distinct method+arity paths; the literal `/options`,`/export`,`/import-template` GETs are all declared BEFORE any `/:id` GET (so `sessions` is never captured as `id="sessions"`), and the single-segment `bulk-*` routes don't collide with the 2/3-seg `/:id/...`. Envelope shapes consistent: self+admin list → bare `SessionInfo[]`; revoke → `{ ok:true }` (controller `res.json({ok:true})`) — matches the module's existing `{ok:true}` convention. SDK matches endpoints exactly: `auth.sessions(currentJti?)`→`GET /auth/sessions[?currentJti=…]` (URL-encoded), `auth.revokeSession(jti)`→POST; `users.sessions(id)`/`users.revokeSession(id,jti)`→the `/users/:id/...` pair; all typed `SessionInfo[]`/`{ok:true}`. Admin controller handlers read `req.params['id']` — consistent with the `:id` param the users router declares; self revoke reads `req.params['jti']` on `/sessions/:jti/revoke`. Mobile/ADR-0012: device label now CARRIED FORWARD across rotation (refresh re-issues with `{deviceId:row.deviceId, deviceInfo:row.deviceInfo}` instead of nulls) — a behavior IMPROVEMENT (sessions keep identity across refreshes), no contract field removed/changed; `ip`/`current` are additive.
  - **(3) DB — migration 0028 forward-only + idempotent + triple-write VERIFIED LIVE.** Two `ALTER … ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` (re-runnable). `ip inet` (nullable — null for pre-slice-6 rows, correct). `last_used_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now()`: adding a NOT-NULL col with a `now()` (volatile) default to a populated table backfills every existing row with the migration-time `now()` — **safe (no NULL-violation, no failure), and on PG ≥11 it's a metadata-only fast add for the default** though `now()` is evaluated per-existing-row at backfill; at this table's volume (rotating refresh tokens) immaterial. `COALESCE(jti=$2,false)` correctly null-handles a missing `currentJti` (admin path passes `null` → every row `current=false`; test-proven all-false without the param). `ip::text` cast is SAFE — `inet`→`text` is a lossless built-in cast, returns the canonical address string (or null). Active-session predicate `revoked_at IS NULL AND expires_at > now()` matches the existing token-validity definition (0009). **Triple-write CONFIRMED LIVE (I queried both containers):** test `crm2_test`@:5433 AND dev `crm2_dev`@:54329 both show `ip inet` (nullable) + `last_used_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now()` — exact type/nullability/default parity with the file. No new index needed: existing `idx_auth_refresh_user (user_id)` (0009) backs the `WHERE user_id=$1` list/revoke scan; `ORDER BY last_used_at DESC` is an in-mem top-N over one user's few sessions (not a 157k-class table — index ratchet N/A).
  - **(4) Quality / conventions — CLEAN.** Grep of added diff lines = ZERO `eslint-disable`/`console.*`/`: any`/`TODO`/`FIXME`; the `no-warning-comments` `temp` ban is respected (no standalone `temp` token in any added comment). No magic numbers in the business layer. Scope SURGICAL (Karpathy) — 9 files, every changed line traces to the slice (repo: insert/find/+2 new methods; service: ip threading + device-carry-forward + list/revoke; controller: 4 handlers; auth+users routes: the 4 routes; SDK: SessionInfo + 4 leaf methods + count bump). Matches the auth-module pattern exactly (mirrors `mfaAdminDisable`/`setPassword` param-handling and the `{ok:true}` write shape). No adjacent "improvements," no speculative config.
  - **Gates GREEN (ran them myself, DATABASE_URL=…:5433/crm2_test):** **auth.api 28/28 PASS** incl. all **7 new session tests** (list-2-devices+ip+excludes-revoked; `?currentJti` flags exactly the caller's row; unknown/already-revoked→404; **IDOR: cross-user revoke→404 + victim untouched**; admin list+revoke 200; admin route→403 for MANAGER; self routes→401 unauth). **SDK client.test 7/7 PASS** (the `toBe(93)` call-count assertion holds: 89+4). **API `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0.** (Single-file coverage threshold "RED" is the documented false-RED — running one test file collapses global coverage; the figure is real at 28/28.)
  - **FLAG #1 (LOW-sev, PRE-EXISTING class — record, not block):** an AUTHENTICATED user passing a NON-uuid jti to `POST /auth/sessions/:jti/revoke` (or admin a non-uuid `:id`) hits `WHERE jti=$1` on a `uuid` column → PG `22P02 invalid input syntax for type uuid` → **500**, not a clean 404/400. NOT a new regression: identical to every existing uuid-param route in the module (`mfaAdminDisable`, `setPassword`, `unlock`, etc. all pass the raw param straight to a uuid `WHERE` with no format guard). The IDOR property is unaffected (a VALID-uuid foreign jti still returns 404). Harden module-wide later with a uuid-format guard (→400) or a `22P02`→404 map; out of scope for a surgical slice.
  - **FLAG #2 (LOW-sev, carried from Slice-4/5 — `req.ip` behind nginx):** `app.ts` does NOT call `app.set('trust proxy', …)`. In prod behind nginx, `req.ip` will be the proxy's socket address (e.g. `127.0.0.1`), not the real client IP — so the captured session `ip` is misleading until trust-proxy is configured. This is a DEPLOY-CONFIG gap, not a code defect in this slice (the column + plumbing are correct); the value is cosmetic/informational (sessions are keyed by jti, not ip — no security decision reads `ip`). **Disposition: noted FLAG, NOT a BLOCK.** Set `trust proxy` to the nginx hop count (and confirm nginx sends `X-Forwarded-For`) at GA so the session IP is truthful; pairs with the Slice-4 "no IP/global rate-limit" carry (same trust-proxy prerequisite).
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit.** No must-fix. Carries: (a) module-wide uuid-param format guard (FLAG #1, low-sev, pre-existing); (b) configure `trust proxy` + verify `X-Forwarded-For` before prod so session `ip` is the real client (FLAG #2, deploy-config). OBSERVATION (carried, FE-wide, unchanged): admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered (server-side 403 is the boundary).

- **2026-06-10 — User-Management parity Slice 7: INFRA — object storage (S3) + transactional email (SMTP), config-gated deferred-activation (NEW deps `@aws-sdk/client-s3`+`@aws-sdk/s3-request-presigner`+`nodemailer`; ADR-0021; migration `0029_user_profile_photo.sql` adds `users.profile_photo_key text`; profile-photo upload + one-time-password email). Panel: CEO/Quality + Security + API-Contract + DB. PER-LENS: Security PASS · API-Contract PASS · DB PASS · Quality/Governance PASS. OVERALL VERDICT: PASS — cleared to commit. 3 LOW-sev FLAGs, no BLOCK.** Re-audited the full `git diff` + every new file adversarially (storage/mail/image platform seams, users service/repo/controller/routes, config schema, ADR, ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES, SDK, FE UserPhoto) against the two new dependencies + file-upload + email attack surface.
  - **(1) Security — SOUND.** **Type validation is by MAGIC BYTES, not the declared Content-Type** (`platform/image.ts` `detectImage` reads leading bytes; the route's client-sent content-type is never trusted — `apiUpload` even sends `application/octet-stream`). A renamed `.exe`/script or text blob is rejected 400 INVALID_IMAGE before it reaches storage (test-proven: `send(Buffer.from('hello'))`→400, `puts.size==0`). **SVG/polyglot: SVG is NOT an accepted type** (only PNG/JPEG/WebP magic), so the classic stored-XSS-via-SVG vector is closed; and the read path serves bytes from a **presigned S3 URL on the bucket origin**, never inline off the app origin, so even a crafted polyglot can't execute in the app's security context. **Object key is 100% server-minted** — `users/<uuid-id>/<randomUUID()>.<ext>` where `id` is UUID-regex-validated by `parseId` and `ext` comes from the magic-byte table (a fixed allow-list `png|jpg|webp`), NOT from the filename — **no path-traversal / no user-controlled key segment**. **put-before-db-write ordering is the SAFE direction**: bytes land in storage, THEN `setPhotoKey` persists; if the DB write throws, the freshly-PUT object is an orphan (harmless, GC-able by bucket lifecycle) — the alternative (DB-first) would leave a key pointing at a missing object (a broken photo), which is worse. Previous-object cleanup is best-effort AFTER the successful key swap. **OTP-in-plaintext-email is an ACCEPTED risk**: it is a forced-change one-time password (`password_must_change=true` set in the same call), single-use, immediately rotated on first login — industry-standard for admin-minted credentials; the alternative (reset-link) is a larger flow deferred. **SSRF via S3_ENDPOINT: NOT user-reachable** — `S3_ENDPOINT` is an operator-set env var (MinIO/S3-compatible host), never request-derived; no endpoint/region/bucket value crosses the request boundary. **Mail failure neither leaks nor blocks**: `SmtpMailer.send` is wrapped in try/catch, logs only `to`+`subject`+`err.message` (never the password — the OTP is only in `msg.text`, which is NOT logged), returns `false`; `generateTempPassword` still returns the plaintext to the admin regardless (best-effort `emailed` flag) — test-proven (no-email user → `emailed:false`, password still returned). Both photo routes correctly gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.USER_MANAGE)` (test-proven: BACKEND_USER → 403 on both POST photo and GET photo-url).
  - **(2) Deferred-activation — CORRECT.** Unconfigured storage → **clean 503** (`disabledStorage` rejects with `AppError(SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,'STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED')`, never a 500 — test-proven both at the provider level and end-to-end HTTP 503). `remove` on the disabled provider is a **no-op** (resolves) so the orphan-cleanup path never explodes when storage is off. Unconfigured mail → `disabledMailer` logs-and-skips, returns `false`, **never throws**; `generateTempPassword` still returns the password (test-proven). **AWS SDK + nodemailer are TRULY lazy**: both live behind `await import(...)` INSIDE the real provider factory, which is only constructed when `storageConfigured()/mailConfigured()` is true — an unconfigured deployment (the default `STORAGE_BACKEND='local'`, no `SMTP_HOST`) constructs the disabled provider and **never executes the dynamic import**, so the large `@aws-sdk` client tree is never loaded into the process. Factory results are cached; `setStorage/setMailer(null)` resets the cache (test seam mirrors `setPool`).
  - **(3) API-contract — CORRECT + additive (ADR-0011).** Route ordering under `/users/:id/*` is collision-free: the new `POST /:id/photo` (2-seg) and `GET /:id/photo-url` (2-seg, distinct literal suffix) don't collide with `/:id/password`, `/:id/sessions` (2-seg, different literal), `/:id/sessions/:jti/revoke` (3-seg), or the single-segment statics (`/options`,`/export`,`/import-template`,`/bulk-*`) which are all declared before the `/:id` routes. `raw({type:()=>true, limit:'6mb'})` runs ONLY on the photo POST (per-route), and global `express.json()` skips the `application/octet-stream` body, so the raw bytes reach the handler intact — same proven transport as `/import`. NEW error codes `STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED`+`INVALID_IMAGE` added to `ERROR_CODES`; `SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE:503` added to `HTTP_STATUS`. SDK matches: `users.photoUrl(id)`→`GET /users/:id/photo-url`; `TempPasswordResponse.emailed:boolean` is an **additive** field (mobile/unknown-field-tolerant clients ignore it; no `/api/v2` bump). No contract field removed or changed.
  - **(4) DB — migration 0029 forward-only + idempotent.** Single `ALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS profile_photo_key text` — re-runnable, no backfill issue (`text`, **nullable**, NULL = no photo, correct). `setPhotoKey`'s correlated subquery is correct: `UPDATE users u SET profile_photo_key=$2 FROM (SELECT profile_photo_key FROM users WHERE id=$1) prev WHERE u.id=$1 RETURNING prev.profile_photo_key AS previous_key` — the `prev` subselect snapshots the OLD value **before** the SET takes effect (Postgres evaluates the FROM-subquery against the pre-update snapshot), so `previousKey` is the genuinely-previous object key (test-proven: replace → old key appears in `removed`). Returns `null` when the user row is absent (no FROM-row → no result row). **TRIPLE-WRITE NOT verifiable in this sandbox (DBs not booted) — implementer MUST confirm `profile_photo_key text` (nullable) lands in file + dev `crm2_dev`@:54329 + test `crm2_test`@:5433 before commit** (the prompt asserts the gate is green incl. 436 api tests, which requires a migrated DB — so this is presumed done, but record it).
  - **(5) Quality/governance — CLEAN.** **ADR-0021 present + sound** (context/decision/consequences/alternatives all addressed: stub-only, bytea-in-PG, and SES-SDK alternatives each rejected with reasons; both deps justified as audited zero-business-logic libraries, same reasoning that admitted `jose`/`exceljs`). **ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES updated** with both rows (S3 pair + nodemailer), owner=CTO(ADR-0021), config-gating + best-effort posture noted; `@types/nodemailer` added as devDep. Grep of the new/changed non-SQL files = ZERO `eslint-disable` / ZERO `console.*` / ZERO `: any` — the lazy dynamic imports are typed via `ReturnType<typeof loadSdk>`/`typeof transport` (no `any` leaks; the narrowed `env.S3_* as string` casts are guarded by `storageConfigured()` upstream, documented in-file). Image constants (`MAX_IMAGE_BYTES`, magic-byte tables) correctly live in `platform/image.ts` to keep them out of the magic-number-linted business layer (service references the named export). `no-warning-comments` `temp` ban respected — no standalone `temp` token in any added comment (the `generateTempPassword`/`temporaryPassword` identifiers are code, not comments; the comments say "one-time password"). Scope SURGICAL — every changed line traces to the slice; matches existing module patterns (`setPool`-style seams, `{url}` envelopes, raw-body transport mirrored from import).
  - **Gates: PROMPT asserts GREEN (typecheck/lint/format/no-suppressions/boundaries + api 436 + sdk 77 + build).** I could NOT independently boot the DBs in this sandbox, so the 14 DB-bound new tests (8 platform storage/mail + 6 users.api photo/email) and the live triple-write are taken on the prompt's assertion — the test code was reviewed line-by-line and is well-shaped (recording fake storage/mailer via the injectable seams, 503/400/404/403 paths, replace-removes-old, emailed-true/false). Implementer: confirm `pnpm verify` green with the DB wired + triple-write before commit.
  - **FLAG #1 (LOW-sev, real — record, not block): WebP magic-byte check is incomplete.** `image.ts` matches WebP on the 4-byte RIFF header `[0x52,0x49,0x46,0x46]` ("RIFF") ONLY — it does **not** verify the `WEBP` FourCC at byte offset 8. RIFF is a shared container header (WAV, AVI also start `RIFF...`), so a `.wav`/`.avi` file would pass validation and be stored with `Content-Type: image/webp`. Impact is LOW (the stored object is served via a presigned URL off the bucket origin, not inline on the app origin, so it's a "broken image," not stored-XSS; and the uploader is already a USER_MANAGE admin), but it defeats the stated "reject spoofed file" intent. **Suggested fix (one line):** for the WebP entry, also assert `bytes[8]===0x57 && bytes[9]===0x45 && bytes[10]===0x42 && bytes[11]===0x50` ("WEBP") — i.e. give the WebP type a second magic segment at offset 8, or special-case it in `detectImage`.
  - **FLAG #2 (LOW-sev, deploy-config — carried class): `MAIL_FROM`/SMTP-auth secrecy + SPF/DKIM at GA.** When SMTP is activated, the OTP email is sent in plaintext over the relay; ensure the relay enforces TLS (`SMTP_SECURE`/STARTTLS) and the `MAIL_FROM` domain has SPF/DKIM so the OTP mail isn't spoofable/junked. `SMTP_PASSWORD` is operator env (not logged). Pure deploy-config, no code defect.
  - **FLAG #3 (LOW-sev, pre-existing class — carried from Slice 6): non-uuid `:id` on the new photo routes.** `parseId` UUID-validates `:id` and 400s a malformed id BEFORE any DB/storage call, so the photo routes are actually SAFER than the older uuid-param routes (sessions/password/unlock) that pass the raw param to a uuid `WHERE` and can 500 on `22P02`. No new exposure; noted only to confirm the new routes don't widen the carried module-wide gap (they don't — they close it for themselves).
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit.** No must-fix. Recommended (non-blocking): harden the WebP magic check (FLAG #1, ~1 line) and confirm the live triple-write + DB-bound test suite green before commit. Carries: TLS/SPF/DKIM on the mail relay at GA (FLAG #2); module-wide uuid-param guard already self-satisfied here (FLAG #3). OBSERVATION (carried, FE-wide, unchanged): admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered (server-side 403 is the boundary).

- **2026-06-10 · Epic F Slice 1 — data-scope seam + case-list hierarchy visibility (uncommitted; `platform/scope/**` new + `modules/cases/{repository,service,controller}.ts` + tests).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: PASS — cleared to commit** with ONE documented follow-up (case DETAIL still unscoped — see BLOCK-class analysis → ruled FOLLOW-UP for this slice).
  - **What it does (verified):** closes the `cases.list` UNSCOPED gap. New seam `platform/scope/repository.ts` (`getScopedUserIds`/`resolveScope`, DB half) + `platform/scope/index.ts` (pure builders `scopeUserIdsParam`/`appendScopeConditions`). `cases/repository.ts:232-240` composes `(cs.created_by = ANY($p) OR EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct WHERE ct.case_id=cs.id AND ct.assigned_to = ANY($p)))` into the list WHERE; `service.ts` resolves scope from `actor`; `controller.ts` threads `actor(req)` (server-trusted `req.auth`) into `list`. `assignableUsers` refactored to reuse `getScopedUserIds`.
  - **(1) SECURITY — PASS. Real boundary, not bypassable.** Scope derives ENTIRELY from server-side `req.auth` (userId + signed-JWT `role`, jwt.ts:51 `p['role'] as Role`), never from client query/body → no param-injection bypass. The SAME `clause` string + SAME `params` array feed BOTH the COUNT (`repository.ts:244-248`) and the items query (`:251-256`) — proven internally consistent by the new test (`cases.api.test.ts:573-575`: unrelated agent `items.length === totalCount === 0`). **No empty-scope fall-through to all-rows:** empty `userIds=[]` is pushed as-is and `col = ANY('{}'::uuid[])` matches zero rows (index.ts:13-14 documents this; the EXISTS leg also yields false) → fail-CLOSED. SUPER_ADMIN bypass correct & narrow: `getScopedUserIds` returns `undefined` → `resolveScope` returns `{}` → `scopeUserIdsParam` returns `null` → NO clause pushed (only for SA). `created_by`-based visibility is INTENDED (a creator sees their own case even if low-role) and is bounded to the actor's own id-set, not a leak. **Cyclic `reports_to` cannot infinite-loop:** the recursive CTE is depth-capped at `SUBTREE_DEPTH_CAP=16` via `WHERE s.depth < $2` (repository.ts:38) — a cycle terminates at 16 levels (fail-safe, not fail-open). Unknown/future role on `req.auth.role` falls through `getScopedUserIds` to `[self]` (fail-closed); the controller default `?? 'FIELD_AGENT'` is also self-only.
  - **(2) `assignableUsers` REFACTOR PARITY — PASS (behavior preserved exactly).** Old per-role SQL vs new `base + id = ANY($1::uuid[])`: SA → unchanged (`base ORDER BY name`, no id filter). MANAGER → old uncapped `WITH RECURSIVE subtree` vs new `getScopedUserIds` (same recursion, now depth-capped 16) — id-set identical for any real org (<16 deep); the cap is a strict-safety improvement (old version would infinite-loop on a `reports_to` cycle — latent bug now removed), NOT a regression. TEAM_LEADER → old `reports_to = $1` (direct reports, excludes self) vs new self+direct-reports id-set; the shared `base` filters `role IN ('FIELD_AGENT','KYC_VERIFIER')` so the TL's own row (role TEAM_LEADER) is filtered out → **net result identical**. FA/KYC/BACKEND → old `return []` vs new early `if (role !== MANAGER && !== TEAM_LEADER) return []` → identical, and the empty-pool path never even hits the DB. Existing parity test (`cases.api.test.ts:450`, mgr→tl→fa 2-level subtree) passes.
  - **(3) DB/SQL — PASS.** EXISTS subquery is CORRELATED on `ct.case_id = cs.id` → semi-join, zero row multiplication, safe inside `count(*)` (the LEFT JOIN to `case_applicants pa is_primary` is already partial-unique, so the count FROM never multiplies). `$p` placeholder reuse correct: `scopeUserIdsParam` pushes the array ONCE and both legs reference the same `$n::uuid[]`. `= ANY('{}'::uuid[])` = no rows (empty-scope semantics, documented). All values bound (`params.push` + `$n`); the only interpolated tokens are `sortColumn`/`sortOrder`, whitelisted in the service `PageSpec.sortMap` (unchanged) → no injection. Columns verified present in the live test DB: `cases.created_by`, `case_tasks.assigned_to` (has index `idx_case_tasks_assigned`, migration 0010_cases.sql:71 — EXISTS is index-supported), `users.reports_to`. sort/filter maps untouched.
  - **(4) ARCHITECTURE — PASS.** DB access (`platform/db` `query`) lives ONLY in `scope/repository.ts` (matches the `repository\.ts$` allowlist in `.dependency-cruiser.cjs:26` `db-access-only-in-repositories` — this is the rule that forced the index/repository split); `scope/index.ts` is PURE (imports only the `Scope` type, re-exports). `controller.ts` imports only the `Actor` TYPE from `scope/index.js`, never the repository → `controller-not-to-repository` (`:15-19`) satisfied. Depth cap is a NAMED constant `SUBTREE_DEPTH_CAP` (not a magic number) and lives in `platform/scope/repository.ts`, outside the `modules/**` magic-number-linted business layer (eslint.config.js:55-66). Single chokepoint: every list path resolves scope through `resolveScope`/`getScopedUserIds`. SURGICAL — every changed line traces to the slice.
  - **(5) COVERAGE GAP — case DETAIL + task reads are NOT scoped (only the list is).** `GET /cases/:id` → `svc.get` → `findById` (`repository.ts:260-272`) has NO scope clause; the route guard is `CASE_VIEW` permission ONLY (`routes.ts`). So a scoped user who knows/guesses a case UUID outside their hierarchy CAN fetch it (header + applicants + tasks) — an **IDOR-class read leak on detail**. Tasks are read only via `TASK_VIEW_BY_CASE` inside `findById` (no standalone task-list endpoint exists in `modules/`), so they inherit the same detail gap, nothing separate. **RULING: FOLLOW-UP, not a BLOCK for Slice 1** — (a) the slice's stated scope is the LIST gap (`cases.list` was the unscoped surface any user hit by default; detail requires guessing a v4 UUID, far higher bar); (b) closing detail is a clean, isolated next step (add `scope` to `findById` + 404-not-403 on out-of-scope to stay IDOR-safe — mirror the `validateTaskRecordAccess` pattern noted in the backend-review epic); (c) no regression — detail was equally unscoped before this slice. **MUST track as Slice 2 / immediate follow-up; do NOT ship the epic to prod with detail open.**
  - **Gates (FRESH RUN, this sandbox, DB on :5433 `crm2_test`): ALL GREEN.** `pnpm typecheck` clean; `pnpm lint` (eslint) clean; `pnpm format` (prettier --check) clean; `pnpm no-suppressions` clean (208 files); `pnpm boundaries` 0 errors (13 pre-existing orphan warnings — config/e2e files, none scope-related); **`pnpm test` (api) = 445 passed / 20 files, coverage thresholds met.** The prompt's known unrelated :5433-pollution flake (verification-units export) did NOT occur this run.
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit.** No MUST-FIX inside the slice's scope. **ONE tracked follow-up (HIGH priority, NOT a commit blocker for the list slice, IS a pre-prod blocker for the epic): scope case DETAIL `findById` + task reads (FLAG #5) — return 404 (not 403) on out-of-scope to stay IDOR-safe.** Recommended verification before merge: re-run `pnpm verify` in CI against the seeded DB. No new carries; standing FE observation (admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered; server-side 403 is the boundary) unchanged.

- **2026-06-10 · Epic F Slice 2 — field-territory assignment tables + API (uncommitted; `db/v2/migrations/0030_user_territory_assignments.sql` + `modules/territoryAssignments/{repository,service,controller,__tests__}` new · `modules/users/routes.ts` +5 routes · `packages/access/permissions.ts` +`TERRITORY_ASSIGN` · `packages/sdk/{userAssignments.ts new,client.ts,client.test.ts,index.ts}`).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: PASS WITH ONE FLAG — cleared to commit; the FLAG (target-user not subtree-scoped for MANAGER) is a documented pre-Slice-3 follow-up, mirrors the Slice-1 detail-IDOR carry, and is NOT a commit blocker for the tables/API slice.**
  - **What it does (verified):** lets SUPER_ADMIN + MANAGER assign a FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER a field territory (pincodes + areas) for slice-3 scope consumption. Two append tables (`user_pincode_assignments`/`user_area_assignments`, both `user_id uuid FK users ON DELETE CASCADE` + `{pincode,area}_id int FK locations`, `is_active`, `assigned_by`, `uq(user_id,*_id)`). Five routes under `/users/:id/territory[/pincodes|/areas[/:id]]`, all gated `TERRITORY_ASSIGN`, delegating to `territoryController`. Every mutation returns the fresh `UserTerritory` (joined city/state). So a MANAGER may read/mutate territory for ANY user uuid — including a FA outside their `reports_to` subtree, another MANAGER, or a SUPER_ADMIN — if they obtain/guess the v4 UUID. This is the FIRST `/users/:id` route ever granted below SUPER_ADMIN (all existing `:id` routes are `USER_MANAGE`=SA-only, and MANAGER lacks `USER_VIEW`/`USER_MANAGE` so has no in-app way to enumerate other users' ids → bar is "guess a v4 UUID", same threat-class as the Slice-1 detail-IDOR carry). **RULING: FOLLOW-UP for Slice 3 (scope-consumption), not a BLOCK for Slice 2 (tables+API)** — (a) the fix is isolated and the primitive already exists: in the controller/service, resolve `getScopedUserIds(actor)` and 404 (not 403, to stay IDOR-safe) when `:id ∉ scope` for non-SA, exactly mirroring the `validateTaskRecordAccess` / Slice-1 FLAG-#5 pattern; (b) no data leak of OTHER domains — only territory rows of the named user; (c) territory is inert until slice-3 reads it. **MUST track; do NOT enable MANAGER territory-assign in prod until target-scoping lands.**
  - **(2) DB — PASS.** Migration forward-only + idempotent: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` ×2, uq constraints added under `pg_constraint` name-guards (`uq_user_pincode`/`uq_user_area`), `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` ×2 — re-runnable against the accumulating test DB. A bad locations id → FK 23503 → `mapWriteError` → 400 `INVALID_REFERENCE` (asserted `:62-68`); `mapWriteError` mirrors the users/cpv pattern exactly. uq prevents dupes. `GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY` PK. **Triple-write (file + dev + test DB) NOT verifiable in this sandbox — SSH tunnels occupy :5432/:5433 and the local docker `crm_postgres` is `acs_db` (prod-shaped); I did NOT run live migrate/truncate to avoid the tunnel-collision risk. Harmless for slice 2 (storage only); slice 3 (scope read) must decide pincode-match semantics (by-id vs by-string) and the comment should be corrected to match whatever lands. - **2026-06-10 · Epic F Slice 3 — case verification-location + field-territory scope EXPANSION (uncommitted; `db/v2/migrations/0031_cases_location.sql` new · `packages/sdk/src/cases.ts` +pincodeId/areaId · `apps/api/src/modules/cases/repository.ts` shared `caseScopePredicate` on list+findById + create-stores-location · `apps/api/src/platform/scope/repository.ts` Scope +pincodeIds/areaIds, `resolveScope` loads territory for FIELD_AGENT/KYC only, `getTerritoryIds` · cases.api `data scope` +1 test).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + DB + API-Contract. **OVERALL: PASS — cleared to commit. No BLOCK, no MUST-FIX. Slice 3 also CLOSES the carried Slice-1 detail-IDOR follow-up (findById is now scoped).** Re-audited the full `git diff` adversarially, traced every load-bearing fact at source, and ran the gates myself (incl. a fresh-DB full api run on a throwaway DB) rather than trust the brief.
  - **What it does (verified):** a case gains optional `pincode_id`/`area_id` (`locations` FK). `resolveScope` now appends the actor's assigned territory ids — but ONLY for `FIELD_AGENT`/`KYC_VERIFIER` (`scope/repository.ts:84-88`); all other roles get `{userIds}` with no territory keys. The new module-level `caseScopePredicate(params, scope)` (`repository.ts`) builds ONE `(hierarchy OR pincode-leg OR area-leg)` group, reused by BOTH `list` (COUNT+items) and `findById`. Net effect: a field agent ALSO sees UNASSIGNED cases located in their pincodes/areas (intended visibility EXPANSION per v1).
  - **(1) SECURITY — PASS (the load-bearing property is sound on all four sub-probes).**
    - **(a) No accidental MANAGER/TL/BE territory expansion — CONFIRMED.** `resolveScope` gates the territory load behind `actor.role === 'FIELD_AGENT' || 'KYC_VERIFIER'` (`scope/repository.ts:84`). MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER never receive `pincodeIds`/`areaIds`, so for them `caseScopePredicate` emits ONLY the hierarchy leg (`length>0` guards skip the territory parts) — zero over-grant. `resolveScope` is the sole producer of `Scope` consumed here.
    - **(b) OR-composition is not an all-rows leak — CONFIRMED.** Each territory leg is `cs.pincode_id = ANY($n::int[])`; an EMPTY territory array is NEVER pushed (the `if (scope.pincodeIds && length>0)` guard), so the degenerate `ANY('{}')` case cannot arise here at all. And even if it did, `= ANY('{}')` matches NOTHING (not all-rows) — verified vs the `scopeUserIdsParam` doc invariant (`scope/index.ts:13-14`). A field agent with NO territory → no territory legs → hierarchy(self)-only → sees only own created/assigned cases. **Test-proven LIVE:** `faOut` (no territory) does NOT see the in-pin case (list) and gets 404 on detail; `faIn` (granted the pin) sees it (list) + 200 (detail).
    - **(c) SUPER_ADMIN still bypasses — CONFIRMED.** `resolveScope(SA)` → `{}` (`scope/repository.ts:80` via `getScopedUserIds`→undefined); `caseScopePredicate` calls `scopeUserIdsParam` which returns `null` for `userIds===undefined`, so the predicate returns `''` BEFORE any territory leg is even considered → no WHERE clause appended (list) / no `AND` (findById). SA sees all. (SA also never carries territory keys regardless.)
    - **(d) Detail honors territory identically + stays IDOR-safe — CONFIRMED.** `findById` composes `AND ${scopePred}` from the SAME shared helper; a row matching NEITHER hierarchy NOR territory → `rows[0]` undefined → `return null` → controller 404 `CASE_NOT_FOUND`. Out-of-scope == non-existent (no 403 oracle). **This CLOSES the Slice-1 FLAG-#5 carry (detail was previously unscoped); the IDOR-class detail read leak is now sealed and test-asserted (faOut→404).**
  - **(2) DB / SQL — PASS.** Param-push order correct: `caseScopePredicate` first calls `scopeUserIdsParam` (pushes the uuid[] → reused for both hierarchy legs as `$ph`), THEN conditionally pushes pincode[] / area[] arrays, each immediately consuming `params.length` for its `$n` — placeholders never cross-bind. The helper is the SINGLE clause used in list COUNT, list items, AND findById (true DRY; brief's "consistency" requirement met). Injection-safe: arrays bound as params with explicit `::int[]` / `::uuid[]` casts, never string-interpolated; column names are literals. `cs.pincode_id`/`area_id` are `integer` and `locations.id` is `integer GENERATED … IDENTITY` (`0004_locations.sql:10`) so the `::int[]` cast and the FK type both match exactly — no cast-500 risk (the uuid-500 lesson does not bite here; ints are the right type). Migration 0031 is forward-only + idempotent (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` ×2, `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_cases_pincode`); both FKs reference `locations(id)` correctly; consistent with the established "a `locations` row = (pincode,area) pair" v2 model and with the 0030 assignment-table FKs. Correlated `EXISTS` on `case_tasks` (unchanged leg) keeps COUNT row-multiplication-free.
  - **(3) CORRECTNESS — PASS.** Operator-precedence is safe: the whole predicate is wrapped `(${parts.join(' OR ')})` — one parenthesized OR-group — and `list` joins it to other clauses with ` AND `, so it ANDs as a unit and cannot leak past per-column filters; `findById` prefixes `AND ` to the already-parenthesized group. `caseScopePredicate` returns `''` for SA (ph===null) AND for `!scope` (undefined) — both call-sites guard `if (scopePred)` / ternary, so an empty string never produces a dangling `WHERE`/`AND`. Field-agent-with-no-territory → hierarchy-only (verified above). Create path stores `pincode_id`/`area_id` (`$6`/`$7`) with `?? null` so omitted location → NULL → case is hierarchy/assignment-scoped only (a NULL `pincode_id` can never match `= ANY(...)`), exactly the documented semantics.
  - **(4) API / QUALITY — PASS.** `pincodeId`/`areaId` are `positiveInt.optional()` (`packages/sdk/src/cases.ts:146-147`; `positiveInt = z.number().int().positive()`) — additive + backward-compatible, no `/api/v2` bump, ADR-0011 honored (existing CreateCase callers unaffected). The `CREATE_NEW`-rationale `.refine` is untouched and still fires (its predicate is independent of the new fields). No `any`, no `eslint-disable`, no magic numbers (the `::int[]` cast is a SQL literal, not a magic number); `caseScopePredicate` is the single shared clause (DRY across list COUNT/items + findById). DB access stays in the repository; territory load stays in `scope/repository.ts` (clean layering). Surgical — every changed line traces to the slice.

Runs on BOTH add paths AFTER zod-parse, BEFORE any write. Test-asserted (FA target→400, missing uuid→404, `:94-110`).
    - **(c) uuid `:id` validated before any uuid-col query — CONFIRMED.** `targetUserId` regex-rejects → 400 `BAD_REQUEST` (`controller.ts:10-14`), so `users.id`/`user_id` uuid columns are never hit with a malformed id (no pg 22P02→500; asserted `:112-122`). int `:clientId`/`:productId` are `Number.isInteger && > 0` guarded (`intParam`).
    - **(d) No empty-array over-grant + fail-closed — CONFIRMED.** `resolveScope` always sets `clientIds`/`productIds` for a BACKEND_USER (possibly `[]`), but `caseScopePredicate` pushes a leg ONLY `if (scope.clientIds && scope.clientIds.length > 0)` (same for products) — an empty array is NEVER bound, so the degenerate `ANY('{}')` cannot arise (and would match nothing anyway, per the `scope/index.ts` invariant). Empty-portfolio BACKEND_USER → hierarchy(self)-only → sees nothing they didn't create/get assigned. **Test-proven LIVE:** `beNone` (no portfolio) list = `[]` AND detail 404; `beClient` sees ONLY client-A's case; `beProduct` ONLY product-B's (cross-axis isolation both directions, `cases.api.test.ts` Slice-4 test). Detail honors portfolio via the SAME shared predicate (findById; beClient→200, beNone→404 — IDOR-safe, out-of-scope == 404).
    - **(e) SA bypass intact — CONFIRMED.** `resolveScope(SA)` never enters the BACKEND_USER branch, and `caseScopePredicate` returns `''` before any leg when `scopeUserIdsParam` → null. Other roles (MANAGER/TL/FA/KYC) never receive `clientIds`/`productIds` — zero cross-role expansion.
    - **(f) `assignedBy` is server-derived** (`req.auth.userId`), never a request param.
  - **(2) DB / SQL — PASS.** Migration 0032 forward-only + idempotent: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` ×2, uq constraints under `pg_constraint` name-guards (`uq_user_client`/`uq_user_product`), `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` ×2 (`idx_uca_user`/`idx_upra_user`) — exactly the 0030 pattern. FKs: `user_id → users ON DELETE CASCADE` (assignments reaped with the user); `client_id → clients` / `product_id → products` plain RESTRICT (bad id → 23503 → `mapWriteError` → 400 `INVALID_REFERENCE`, test-asserted). Set-based `INSERT…SELECT FROM unnest($2::int[]) ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE SET is_active = true` — fully parameterized, injection-safe, idempotent (re-add no-op asserted). `cs.client_id`/`cs.product_id` are `integer NOT NULL` (`0010_cases.sql:12-13`) so the `::int[]` casts type-match exactly (no cast-500 risk), and BOTH predicate legs ride pre-existing indexes (`idx_cases_client` 0010, `idx_cases_product` 0021) — no new cases index needed. Param-push order in `caseScopePredicate` stays correct: each leg consumes `params.length` immediately after its own push — placeholders never cross-bind across the now-five legs.
  - **(3) CORRECTNESS / QUALITY — PASS.** Raw SQL lives ONLY in repositories (`portfolioAssignments/repository.ts` + the scope read in `platform/scope/repository.ts`, same home as territory); service = zod-parse + eligibility + orchestration; controller = param guards only — clean layering, boundaries-conformant. No `any`, no `eslint-disable`, no magic numbers in service/controller/repository (`FK_VIOLATION`/`UUID_RE`/`PORTFOLIO_ROLE` are named constants; the 1-500 bounds live in the shared SDK `ID_ARRAY` zod, re-parsed server-side — server does not trust the client). Every mutation returns the fresh `UserPortfolio` (joined code/name) — Access-tab single-round-trip contract kept. The OR-composition stays one parenthesized group ANDed as a unit; `''` for SA still short-circuits both call-sites. Surgical: every changed line traces to the slice.
  - **(4) API / SDK — PASS, additive.** SDK adds `users.{portfolio,assignClients,removeClient,assignProducts,removeProduct}` + `UserPortfolio`/`PortfolioItem` + `AssignClients/ProductsSchema` (shared `ID_ARRAY`, `min(1).max(500)`); transport asserted (calls 99→104, `client.test.ts`); no `/api/v2` bump, existing surface untouched (ADR-0011). Route ordering safe: `/:id/portfolio*` are literal-segment paths, same non-collision argument as `/territory` (no `/:id/:x` wildcard precedes them).
  - **Gate (run by orchestrator, treated as green): `pnpm verify` EXIT=0 on a fresh :5433 — api 455 passed (450 + 4 portfolio + 1 cases-scope), sdk 77, logger 4.** This pass was a full static + invariant re-verification of the diff and all untracked files at source.
  - **DISPOSITION: PASS — cleared to commit.** No MUST-FIX. Three NON-blocking notes: (i) remove endpoints skip the eligibility/existence check (DELETE on a missing pair/user is a row-less no-op returning an empty portfolio) — mirrors the territory module exactly, consistent by design, not a leak; (ii) `is_active` is written `true` (re-activation path) but nothing sets it `false` — removes are hard DELETEs, identical to the 0030 territory pattern, harmless latent column; (iii) cross-axis semantics are OR (client-leg OR product-leg), matching the territory pincode-OR-area precedent and test-asserted — flag for the Access-tab UX copy so admins don't assume AND. Pre-commit reminder: apply migration 0032 to dev + remote (triple-write invariant) before/with the commit.

- **2026-06-10 · Access Control 2.0 Slice 1 — roles-as-data foundation (ADR-0022; uncommitted, PURELY ADDITIVE: `db/v2/migrations/0033_roles.sql` new · `modules/access/__tests__/roles.parity.test.ts` new — ZERO modified files).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: PASS — cleared to commit. Same idiom as the 0007 admin seed — fine for fresh/test DBs; matters only if migrations are ever re-applied to a config-edited dev DB after slice-3 admin editing lands.

- **2026-06-10 · Access Control 2.0 Slice 2 — authorize() cutover to DB-backed role attributes + editable role→permission mapping (ADR-0022; uncommitted on top of `bb348f0`).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: PASS — cleared to commit. No BLOCK, no MUST-FIX.** Re-verified every brief claim at source + both live DBs and ran the gate myself: **`pnpm verify` EXIT=0** (typecheck/lint/format/no-suppressions/boundaries/build en route) + explicit re-run of the api suite: **463/463 across 24 files** (458+4 roles.api +1 parity SA-zero-rows), sdk 77 (106-call transport assert held), logger 4. **The whole 463-test suite now flows through DB-backed `authorize()` — that IS the day-0 parity gate, and it is green.**
  - **The cutover is real and total.** `authorize(perm)` = `grantsAll===true || permissions?.includes(perm)` — grep over apps+packages source: **ZERO** `roleHas`/`buildAccessMatrix`/`ACCESS_ROLES`/`AccessRole` references remain (definitions deleted); `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` survives ONLY as the parity-test reference (+1 stale FE comment, `CaseDetailPage.tsx:18`, a slice-4/6 demolition item). Default-deny when attributes absent; enrichment is in the ONE app chain (`testAuth → authenticate → enrichAuth`) and every `authorize()` consumer sits behind it (grepped — no worker/script bypass).
  - **(1) Privilege escalation — day-0 surface PROVEN minimal.** `role.manage` exists in the code catalog but has **0 explicit `role_permissions` rows on BOTH live DBs** (queried :5433 + :54329) — only `grants_all` (SUPER_ADMIN) reaches `PUT /roles/:code/permissions` day-0; MANAGER-403 test-proven. By design (ADR-0022 §5 + the permissions.ts comment), SA *may* grant `role.manage` to another role, after which that role can self-escalate to the full catalog — **role.manage is super-admin-equivalent**; coherent with the ADR, but the slice-5 UI MUST warn on granting it (carried). SA row itself is unlockable-by-API (`grants_all` → 400 ROLE_LOCKED, test-proven) so SA can never lock itself out.
  - **(2) Cache — ordering correct, staleness bounded.** `invalidateRoleCache()` fires AFTER commit (repository.ts:82); wholesale `cache.clear()` is right-sized (≤6 keys). Residual race accepted per spec §8: an in-flight read-through can re-cache the pre-edit set just after invalidation — bounded by the 5s TTL; cross-worker invalidation = GA item (single process today). NOTE (LOW): the cached `permissions` array is shared by reference onto `req.auth` across requests — `readonly string[]` typing blocks compile-time mutation; if any handler ever mutates it, it poisons the cache. Empty `permissions: []` is accepted → role goes dark: INTENDED (default-deny; spec: new roles start at zero perms), audited + reversible. Resolver failure → `next(e)` 500 — honest outage, never a silent 403: correct.
  - **(4) Audit + OCC — sound.** Append-only `audit_log` row (entity 'roles', before/after permission sets, versionAfter) INSIDE the same txn as DELETE+INSERT; OCC CAS on `roles.version` (`WHERE code AND version` → 0 rows → fresh-row 409 STALE_UPDATE / 404 ROLE_NOT_FOUND). The pre-txn `before` read is OCC-consistent: any interleaved commit bumps version and the CAS fails, so a successful write's `before` is provably the set the version covered. 409/404/audit-row all test-proven.
  - **(5) Injection — closed.** Permission writes: catalog allowlist (`INVALID_PERMISSION` 400, test-proven) BEFORE a fully parameterized `unnest($2::text[])`; role code: `^[A-Z][A-Z0-9_]{1,19}$` controller regex (slice-1 F1 ratchet honored on this surface — slice-5 role-create must reuse it) + parameterized everywhere; zod caps the array at 200.

- **2026-06-10 · Access Control 2.0 Slice 3 — generic scope-assignment model: `scope_dimensions` + `role_scope_dimensions` + `user_scope_assignments` + ONE assignment API replacing territory/portfolio (ADR-0022; uncommitted on top of `b52a353`).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: PASS — cleared to commit. Dev DB (:54329/crm2_dev) re-queried: 1 CLIENT + 3 PINCODE rows migrated, all 4 Epic-F tables `to_regclass`→NULL, 7 dimension rows + 6 seed wiring rows, XOR CHECK + both partial uniques live (`\d` inspected).
  - **(1) SQL injection via interpolation — CLOSED.** The only interpolated SQL fragments are `def.catalogTable` (TS union literal `'clients'|'products'|'locations'|'verification_units'`), `def.valueColumn` (`'state'|'city'`) and `def.labelExpr` — all constants from the code-owned registry (`platform/scope/dimensions.ts:30-53`), reachable ONLY through `dimensionDef(code)` lookup (unknown → `undefined` → 400 UNKNOWN_DIMENSION at service.ts:18 BEFORE any SQL). The request-supplied `dimension` string itself is used solely as a bind param (`$2` in repository.ts:108/117, `$2` in assignedEntityIds) or a Map key — never interpolated. ids/values go through `ANY($1::int[])`/`unnest($3::int[])`/`ANY($1::text[])`. GALAXY-400 test-proven.
  - **(2) Duplicate-slip via NULLs / ON CONFLICT targets — SOUND.** `chk_usa_exactly_one_key` (`(entity_id IS NULL) <> (entity_value IS NULL)`) puts every row in EXACTLY one of the two partial unique indexes; within each index all three key columns are NOT NULL, so there is no NULL-uniqueness hole. The upsert conflict targets (`(user_id, dimension_code, entity_id) WHERE entity_id IS NOT NULL` and the value twin, repository.ts:106/115) match the index defs verbatim → correct inference; idempotent re-add (DO UPDATE is_active=true) test-proven. Concurrent double-add lands on the same arbiter — no dup possible.
  - **(3) Data migration — complete + idempotent, heavily exercised.** Column-for-column copy (user_id, entity_id, is_active, assigned_by, created_at); the old tables' `uq_user_*` UNIQUE constraints (0030:28/31, 0032:28/31) guarantee no source dupes; bare `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` is legal against partial-index arbiters. `to_regclass` guards make the re-run-after-drop a clean no-op — and the test harness re-applies ALL migrations per suite (testDb.ts migrate() has no ledger), so 0034 ran ~23× in the green verify, including the recreate(0030/0032-empty)→re-migrate→re-drop cycle.   - **(5) Audit — compliant.** Both writes append inside the SAME `withTransaction` as the mutation (repository.ts:120/144); action `'UPDATE'` is in the 0017 CHECK; `actor_id` is text (the 'unknown' fallback can't violate a type, and is unreachable behind authorize); append-only trigger blocks rewrite. COSMETIC: the add's `before` grouped-snapshot is read in the service just BEFORE the txn opens (service.ts:38), not inside it — benign on an SA-only surface but the brief's "in-txn" wording oversells it; remove's audit carries no `before` (the removed row's identity is in `after.removed`). Old modules wrote NO audit at all — strict improvement.

  - **(7) The no-dangling-refs argument (catalogs never hard-DELETE) — VERIFIED.** Grep of every `DELETE FROM` in api src: exactly 3 (user_scope_assignments owner-scoped remove, user_mfa_secrets, role_permissions replace-set). Zero DELETEs against clients/products/locations/verification_units — the spec §3 accepted-tradeoff (service-side existence check instead of a polymorphic FK) holds. NOTE: the existence check runs in a query BEFORE the insert txn, not "in the same transaction" as spec §3 words it — with soft-delete-only catalogs the TOCTOU is theoretical; record the deviation rather than add ceremony.
  - **(8) VALUE-kind semantics — correct.** `SELECT DISTINCT <col> FROM locations WHERE <col> = ANY($1::text[])` then exact `includes` compare → case-sensitive both ways (consistent: only a value byte-equal to a real locations value passes, and that same value is what's stored/unique-indexed); NULL columns can't match ANY. Atlantis-400 / Maharashtra-ok / kind-mismatch-400 / wired-then-unwired role gating all test-proven. Role wiring is fail-closed double-keyed: `rsd.is_active AND sd.is_active` join (repository.ts:35-36).
  - **LOW findings (none blocking):** (L1) ids > int4 range pass the zod/`Number.isInteger` guards and die in the `::int[]` cast → pg 22003 → 500 (POST entityIds + DELETE :assignmentId) — carried from the old modules' identical shape; SA-only surface; consider `.max(2_147_483_647)` next touch. (L2) `AssignScopeSchema` permits BOTH entityIds+entityValues; the wrong-kind array is silently ignored rather than 400 — add an XOR `.refine`. (L3) no parity assertion between the code registry and the `scope_dimensions` rows (an entity_kind drift would desync validation vs wiring) — one-liner test, fold into slice 4. (L4) DELETE owner-scoping (`AND user_id`) and the cross-user/miss no-op are implemented but untested. COSMETIC: GET/DELETE on a nonexistent user → 200 `{}`/no-op (only POST 404s — old-module parity); reactivation upsert keeps the original `assigned_by`; `is_active=false` is unreachable via this API (remove hard-DELETEs) so the column is vestigial except for migrated rows.
  - **OBSERVATIONS for slices 4–6:** role-change orphans — changing a user's role (FA→BE) leaves PINCODE rows dormant and they'd resurface on change-back; slice-4 `resolveScope` must intersect assignments with the role's ACTIVE dimension wiring (spec §4.3.2 already says so — hold it to that). - **2026-06-10 · Access Control 2.0 Slice 4 — GENERIC SCOPE ENGINE: visibility cutover to role attributes + dimension registry; last role-name demolition in api src (ADR-0022 §4; uncommitted on top of `42de20f`).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract + DB. **OVERALL: FLAG — ONE in-slice MUST-FIX (one line + one test), everything else clean. Commit after the fix.** Re-verified at source, re-ran the gates myself (fresh `crm2_audit` on :5433, 3 full runs), re-queried the dev DB (:54329/crm2_dev).
  - **(1) 🔴 MUST-FIX (HIGH, in-slice): RESTRICT unknown-dimension is fail-OPEN at the composition chokepoint.** `composeScopePredicate` (`platform/scope/index.ts:33-36`) does `const def = dimensionDef(dimension); if (def && values) andParts.push(...)` — a RESTRICT entry whose dimension code is missing from the CODE registry is **silently skipped → the cap is lost → over-grant**, violating the locked fail-closed invariant at the exact seam built to hold it. (The EXPAND loop's skip is the safe direction.) NOT exploitable today: no API writes `scope_dimensions` (grep: zero module INSERT/UPDATE paths), wiring FKs to the 7 code-seeded rows, and the new registry↔catalog lockstep test (scope.test.ts, closes slice-3 L3) pins parity in CI. But it is a live deploy-order/drift landmine: a future migration seeding dimension #8 + RESTRICT wiring before the registry code ships, or a registry removal with wiring rows persisting, silently un-caps every role wired to it — and slice 5 puts wiring behind an admin API. **Minimal fix:** in the restrict loop, `andParts.push(def && values ? def.casePredicate(params, values) : 'FALSE')` + one unit test (`restrict: { GHOST: [1] } → predicate contains FALSE`). One line; do it in this slice.
  - **(2) Over-grant sweep — otherwise CLOSED.** EXPAND-[] is double-guarded (resolveScope only sets `expand` when `values.length>0`; the composer re-checks) → `ANY('{}')` can never appear on the OR side. RESTRICT-[] stays in the scope (`repository.ts` keeps `restrict[dim]=values` unconditionally) → emitted as `= ANY('{}')` → matches nothing — fail-closed cap proven at both layers (scope.test exact-SQL + cases.api RESTRICT E2E zero-assignments→`[]` + detail-404). An assignments/wiring query failure THROWS (rejects the request) — never degrades to uncapped. Unknown role → `getRoleAttributes`→null → `'SELF'` + no wiring → [self], test-proven (`GHOST_ROLE`). Orphan assignments (slice-3 MUST-HOLD) are inert: resolveScope intersects with ACTIVE wiring (`roleDimensionModes` double-keys `rsd.is_active AND sd.is_active`), test-proven (CLIENT row on a FIELD_AGENT ignored). **HELD.**
  - **(3) SQL shape + injection — CORRECT.** Hierarchy leg: userIds pushed ONCE, placeholder reused across `created_by = ANY($n)` and the correlated-EXISTS assignee leg (same bind, no SET-vs-compare type split — the PR-#22 lesson doesn't bite: single context, uuid[] both). Precedence safe: all OR-legs joined inside one paren group, RESTRICT legs ANDed outside — `((hier OR expand…) AND restrict…)`; exact strings asserted in scope.test. Predicate shared by list WHERE + COUNT + findById (repository.ts:261-262/286-287) — IDOR-404 parity preserved. Every fragment originates in the code-owned registry (`dimensions.ts` `casePredicate` + `pushParam`); request/DB strings are only bind params or Map/registry keys, never interpolated.
  - **(4) STATE/CITY semantics — coherent, document for slice 5.** Legs are `EXISTS (… sl.id = cs.pincode_id AND sl.state = ANY($::text[]))`: a case with NULL `pincode_id` (column nullable, 0031) never matches — under EXPAND it simply isn't expanded in; under a RESTRICT geo wiring a location-less case is INVISIBLE even to its creator.   - **(4) Mode×kind matrix — now covered end-to-end.** ID-EXPAND (CLIENT/PRODUCT slice Epic-F-4, PINCODE territory slice 3) · ID-RESTRICT (CLIENT, slice 4) · VALUE-EXPAND (STATE, here) · VALUE-RESTRICT (CITY, here) · task-level EXISTS (VT, here). - **2026-06-11 · Access Control 2.0 Slice 8 — BULK scope-assignment import (template→preview→confirm on the platform import engine) + all-assignments export (uncommitted on `9a6b425`).** Panel: CEO/Quality-Sentinel + Security + API-Contract. **OVERALL: FLAG — ONE MUST-FIX (export gate) before commit; everything else PASS-grade.** Re-ran the gates myself: `pnpm verify` EXIT=0 (fresh :5433) · **api 469/469 (24 files)** · **sdk 77/77** · web build green.   - **(1) 🚨 MUST-FIX (HIGH, security): `GET /users/scope/export` is gated `DATA_EXPORT`, not `ACCESS_SCOPE_ASSIGN` (`users/routes.ts:70`).** Live `role_permissions` re-queried on :5433: MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER all hold `data.export` (0033_roles.sql:65/69/73) → any of them can download the ENTIRE access-control topology (every user's username+name+role+assigned clients/products/pincodes/areas/states/cities/VTs) while the interactive read `GET /:id/scope-assignments` is `ACCESS_SCOPE_ASSIGN` = SA-only, and `exportData` applies NO scope seam (global dump — right for SA, wrong for wider roles). The plan's slice-8 line says verbatim "Gate ACCESS_SCOPE_ASSIGN" (2026-06-10 plan §Slice 8). The slice-1/2 "mirrors users `/export`" precedent does NOT transfer: there the DataGrid the role can already read is the export surface; here NO grid exists and the ONLY read surface is SA-only, so `data.export` *widens* read access — a privilege-asymmetry bypass, reachable from the UI too (FE routes are not permission-gated; a MANAGER on /admin/users gets a 403'd grid but a WORKING "Export Scope" button). Fix = 1 line (`authorize(T)`; optionally `T`+`DATA_EXPORT`). **Companion test gap:** the suite asserts MANAGER import→403 but never MANAGER export — which would be 200 today; add the 403 assert with the fix. Finding deduced from gate+seed+authorize chain (each link source-verified), not live-HTTP-proven.
  - **(2) Injection — PASS.** Every user-controlled value is a bound param (`userIdByUsername`/`locationIdsByPincode`/`locationIdByPincodeArea`/`catalogIdByCode` repository.ts:43-76; `allForExport` LIMIT bound). The only interpolations are `def.catalogTable`/`labelExpr`/`valueColumn` from the code-owned closed `DIMENSIONS` registry (`platform/scope/dimensions.ts` — `DimensionCode` union, never user input). Proto-key probe checked: `dimensionDef('__proto__')` WOULD return truthy `Object.prototype`, but the import path is unreachable (zod `.toUpperCase()` transform → `__PROTO__` → undefined) and the interactive path fail-closes first on the `roleDimensions` wiring check → 400 before any interpolation. LOW carry (pre-existing slice-3/4 code, not this slice): harden `dimensionDef` with `Object.hasOwn` next touch.
  - **(3) Formula injection in export (CWE-1236) — PASS at the platform.** CSV: `escapeCsvCell` (export/format.ts:43-47) prefixes `'` on leading `= + - @ \t \r` then RFC-4180-quotes — usernames/names/labels (user-controlled) all flow through `cell()`→`escapeCsvCell`. XLSX: exceljs 4.4 `addRow` stores plain strings as string cells (a formula requires an explicit `{formula}` object) — never executed. Import side symmetric: `cellRaw` unwraps a formula cell to its cached `result` (text), never evaluates.
  - **(4) Confirm bypasses `service.add` — EQUIVALENT-OR-STRICTER, accepted.** `resolveImportRow` re-runs in BOTH preview and confirm (engine `resolveValid` is mode-shared) and covers everything `service.add` checks: registry (`dimensionDef`), active-user resolution (stricter — `service.add` lets you assign to an INACTIVE user; import's `userIdByUsername` requires `is_active`), role wiring (`roleDimensions`), entity existence (ids come FROM the DB by construction). TOCTOU between the resolve loop and the per-row `repo.add` writes is intra-request (ms) and the same check-then-write class as the interactive path; `repo.add` is idempotent (ON CONFLICT re-activate) + per-row append-audit with `before` snapshot inside one transaction. ACCEPTED. PARITY NOTE (LOW): `catalogIdByCode` has no `is_active` filter → an inactive client/product/VU code resolves and assigns — byte-consistent with interactive `existingIds` (existence-only by documented design: "catalogs deactivate rather than hard-DELETE"), recorded not flagged.
  - **(5) DoS — bounded, accepted with one platform carry.** Body `raw({limit:'10mb'})`; `assertImportable` (<10k rows, IMPORT_JOB_THRESHOLD default 10000) throws 413 BEFORE resolve → worst case ~4 sequential queries/row × 9,999 rows under an SA-only gate; terminates, no pool fan-out (serial awaits). Export: `allForExport` LIMIT-bound at `exportThreshold()` + `assertExportable` on mode=all. CARRY (pre-existing, identical in users/clients imports — not a slice regression): `assertImportable` runs AFTER `parseImportFile`, so exceljs inflates the whole workbook in memory before the row cap (10mb zip can expand ~100:1); fix belongs in the platform engine (streaming reader or row-count short-circuit). LOW: export `mode=current|selected` skip `assertExportable` and silently truncate at the LIMIT instead of 413 (FE only sends mode=all; cosmetic contract wrinkle). LOW: per-row `before = listForUser` in the confirm processor is an N+1 — bounded by the threshold, matches the interactive audit shape, fine.
  - **(6) Audit — PASS.** Confirm writes the permanent `import_log` row (§7: resource `user_scope_assignments`, file_name via `x-filename` → bound text param, totals, duration, actor) + structured logger line; preview writes NOTHING (verified: `runImportPreview` has no processor/log call). Conversely the new statics steal no legitimate traffic (`:id` is uuid-guarded; "scope" can never be a valid id). The in-code comment's claim is verified true.
  - **(8) The 400001→ALL-area-rows semantics + resolution edge cases.** PINCODE cell intentionally fans out to every active `locations` row of that pincode (test-pinned: 2 rows) — the right bulk semantics for the one-row-per-area granularity. ## 2026-06-11 · Pipeline Slice 4 — milestone close-out (CTO review; docs-only)
