## 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS Engine Slice 1 (config backbone) — **PASS**

Audited adversarially (working tree, uncommitted). CTO pre-verified pnpm verify EXIT=0, openapi 202→207, migration triple-written, live :4000 E2E. My job: product/scope/frozen-standards/bugs/the ADR-0015 deviation.

**Scope — clean, no overreach.** Every touched file traces to "config backbone only": mig `0060_report_layouts.sql`, `@crm2/sdk` contract (`reportLayouts.ts`+test+index export+`client.ts` method+`client.test`), the `reportLayouts/` module (repo/service/controller/routes+api test), `app.ts` wiring, `openapi.json`, ADR-0037+spec. NO FE, NO generation, NO `case_data_entries`, NO `v_mis_rows` — exactly slices 2–6 deferred. Karpathy scope test passes.

**ADR-0015 §3 deviation (dedicated `report_layouts` pair vs extending `report_templates`/mig 0008) — SOUND + properly documented.** ADR-0037 §1 states it explicitly, gives the rationale (0008 is a type-keyed narrative-PDF `content`-blob engine; MIS layouts are structured ordered source-bound columns — overloading muddies both), and correctly frames it as implementation-evolution of an Accepted-but-UNBUILT ADR, not a frozen-decision reopen. `report_templates` stays for the deferred CASE_REPORT kind. Not a frozen-standard violation. The spec's own schema block hedged ("decide in ADR-0037; leaning dedicated pair") and the ADR is the authority that resolved it — correct precedence.

**Frozen standards — all honoured.** OCC ADR-0019: `version` col + `requireVersion` (pulled out of the per-entity zod schema so VERSION_REQUIRED stays stable) + `FOR UPDATE`+stale-throw in `update`, `WHERE…version=$4`+`AppError.stale(before)` in `setActive`. RBAC default-deny: every route gates `TEMPLATE_MANAGE` (reads tightened to admin too — deliberate, admin config surface). Repository/service/controller layering mirrors `rates`/`commission_rates`. Pagination/PageSpec sortMap+filterMap whitelist (ORDER BY interpolation is whitelisted — safe, comment present). Append-only audit n/a this slice (config table, created_by/updated_by carried). camelize is global in `db.ts` so snake→camel row mapping is NOT a hand-rolled risk here.

**Spec/owner-decision conformance.** 3 kinds DATA_ENTRY/MIS/BILLING_MIS ✓; config-engine-first ✓; one-active-per-(client,product,kind) via partial unique `WHERE is_active` ✓; NO effective-dating (ADR-0037 §2 — layout is "the active one", not temporally resolved; simpler than 0036, migration correctly OMITS effective_from/to even though the spec's draft schema block listed them — ADR supersedes, consistent) ✓; NO GST/invoice/payout ✓. Perm: spec slice-1 line says "a new report.template.manage" but ADR §5 says REUSE existing `report_template.manage` — code reuses `TEMPLATE_MANAGE` (=`report_template.manage`, granted to SUPER_ADMIN via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`); ADR is authority, no new perm = correct least-surface for an admin config slice. Minor doc drift (spec line vs ADR) — cosmetic, ADR governs.

**Source-binding validation = REAL contract, not theater.** `validateColumnSource` enforces three honest modes: FIXED (`source_ref` ∈ enumerated catalog keys → bad ref 400, tested `not_a_field`), REFLESS (ref MUST be empty → stray ref 400, tested `TAT`+'x'), FREE (non-empty only, deferred to consuming slice — explicitly labelled, not pretending to validate what it can't yet). Wired into the zod `superRefine` so it fires at the API boundary (api test: badFixed→400, strayRef→400) AND the SDK schema (FE will reuse). SDK test asserts every SOURCE_TYPES member has a catalog entry (no orphan enum). The DB CHECK on `source_type` is a second floor under the app validation. This is a genuine allow-list, the single contract the ADR promises.

**OCC / one-active / CRUD logic — no latent bug found.** Probed: (1) deactivate→reactivate-over-new-active raises 23505 on `uq_report_layouts_active` → mapped to 409 REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS — the outer try wraps `before` SELECT + UPDATE so the index violation is caught (api test proves the full deact→new-B→reactivate-A→409 sequence). (2) `update` never touches is_active/kind/client/product so it can't violate the active-unique index; OCC `FOR UPDATE`+version then DELETE+re-INSERT columns inside ONE tx (atomic), `findDetail` after commit. (3) `update`'s `version+1` + `setActive`'s `version+1` both bump, stale replays → 409 (tested). (4) `byConfig` returns null (200) for an unconfigured CPV+kind — a normal answer, not 404 (tested); admin-gated so no cross-scope leak despite no case-scope guard (config object, not case data). (5) `repo.list` takes raw `kind:string` but service `toKind` drops non-enum → undefined → no filter (injection-safe; filter goes through param binding regardless). (6) `insertColumns` `displayOrder ?? i` gives stable order; `ORDER BY display_order, id` deterministic. No reused-bind-param type-conflict class (the 2026-06-04 SEV-1 pattern) — every param distinct.

**Verdict: PASS.** Backbone-only, scope-disciplined, frozen-standards-clean, the ADR-0015 deviation is sound and documented at the right altitude, and the source-binding is a real two-floor contract (zod + DB CHECK) rather than theater. No BLOCK, no must-fix FLAG. Carry-forward (NOT blockers): (a) spec slice-1 perm line ("a new report.template.manage") drifts from ADR §5 (reuse) the code follows — tidy the spec line when convenient; (b) FREE-mode refs (DATA_ENTRY_FIELD/FORM_DATA_PATH/DOC_TYPE_COUNT/COMPUTED) are deferred-validated by design — the consuming slices (3–5) MUST close that floor (e.g. DATA_ENTRY_FIELD must resolve to a real active DATA_ENTRY column key) or the "real contract" weakens; (c) immutable-once-used for DATA_ENTRY layouts is explicitly deferred to slice 3 — currently `update` can replace columns freely, fine while no case holds keyed data, but slice 3 MUST add the in-use guard before data-entry persists.

## 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS ENGINE SLICE 2 (FE Layout Designer) review — NEW `apps/web/src/features/reportLayouts/ReportLayoutsPage.tsx` (577 lines) + 4-line wiring (App route / Layout nav / a11y+viewport e2e), UNCOMMITTED, FE-only consuming audited slice-1 API — VERDICT: **PASS** (0 BLOCK, 2 low FLAG, 0 INFO)

**Owner decisions all honored.** config-engine-first + no-default-format: every layout starts from `blankRow()` (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:58), create POST seeds NO columns, copy says "built from blank, no default format" (:548) — faithful. each-CPV+kind-separate: create binds clientId+productId+kind; edit LOCKS all three via `disabled={isEdit}` (:223,:239,:255); server `uq_report_layouts_active` partial-unique is the real floor, reactivation collision → REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS handled (:474). full designer present: add (:278) / remove (:398) / reorder up-down (:135,:382-391) / source-bind / section / required / type. OCC on all 3 mutating verbs: PUT sends `version` (:160), activate/deactivate send `version` (:466) — STALE_UPDATE handled in both designer (:176) and toggle (:471).

**Perm gate correctly mirrors server (verified both sides).** FE: nav entry `perm:'report_template.manage'` (Layout.tsx:51), page guard `has('report_template.manage')` → access-denied div (:539), and `has()` honors `grantsAll` (:459). Server: EVERY reportLayouts route gates `report_template.manage` (routes.ts:7; api.test:226 proves BACKEND_USER→403). `@crm2/access` maps it to SUPER_ADMIN. No new permission minted. Aligned end-to-end.

**Designer state machine — probed adversarially, no data-integrity bug.** (1) set-state-during-render hydration guard (:111-131) is the legal React derived-state pattern: bounded by `!hydrated`+`setHydrated(true)`, batches into one re-render, and DELIBERATELY does not re-hydrate on background refetch (preserves user edits) — correct. (2) column→payload mapping (:146-158): REFLESS → `sourceRef: undefined` (:152) AND source-type onChange resets `sourceRef:''` (:314) AND `rowError` passes `null` for REFLESS (:194) — triple-safe, server's "REFLESS takes no ref" can't fire. (3) FIXED auto-sets dataType from catalog field (:333-338); REFLESS renders "— derived —" (:357), FREE renders text input w/ per-type placeholder (:349) — source-mode adaptation matches SOURCE_CATALOG modes exactly. (4) `canSave` (:197) requires name + ≥1 row + every-row valid + (edit OR client&product) — gates the button correctly. (5) error mapping (:174-185) covers STALE_UPDATE / REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS / VALIDATION → friendly copy, else raw `e.code`. Confirmed contract shapes live: ApiError.code = `json.error` (sdk.ts:76); server emits `error:'VALIDATION'`@400 (app.ts:115), `STALE_UPDATE`@409 (errors.ts:57), `REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS`@409 (repository.ts:23) — every handled branch real.

**Claimed-done IS wired.** route `/admin/report-layouts`→ReportLayoutsPage (App.tsx:66); nav under ADMINISTRATION (Layout.tsx:51); a11y.spec + viewport.spec gained the page entry (`primary:/New Layout/`). CTO browser-verified :5273 (create persisted, edit hydrates+locks, REFLESS "— derived —", 0 console errors). All SDK symbols barrel-exported (`export * from './reportLayouts.js'` index.ts:17); pnpm verify EXIT=0.

**FLAG-1 (low, UX, server-caught — not blocking).** `canSave`/`rowError` only require `headerLabel.trim()!==''`, but `columnKey` is `r.columnKey || slug(headerLabel)` and `slug()` returns `""` for all-punctuation or non-Latin headers (probed: `"!!!"`→"", `"日本語"`→""). Such a row passes client gating then server zod `columnKey.min(1)` rejects → generic "Some columns are invalid" toast. No bad data lands (server floor holds), but the hint is non-specific and doesn't point at the offending row. Consider a client-side `columnKey` non-empty check in `rowError` so the per-row hint fires inline.

**FLAG-2 (low, UX, server-caught — not blocking).** `canSave` does NOT detect duplicate `columnKey` across rows (two rows slugging to the same key). Server `layoutColumnsSchema` superRefine catches it → VALIDATION → same generic toast, no inline pointer. Same remedy class as FLAG-1; collapse both into a richer client mirror if/when the designer gets polish. `INVALID_REFERENCE` (FK on bad client/product) also falls through to raw `e.code`, but dropdowns are server-fed so it's near-unreachable.

**Verdict: PASS.** Scope-disciplined FE slice — zero backend change, zero new permission, no scope creep (no generation, no template-engine touch). Honors all four owner decisions (config-first / no-default / full-designer / per-CPV+kind-separate). State machine is sound; the two FLAGs are server-caught UX-message gaps, not integrity holes. No must-fix. Carry-forward: the FREE-mode deferred-validation floor (DATA_ENTRY_FIELD/FORM_DATA_PATH/DOC_TYPE_COUNT/COMPUTED) still rides on the consuming generation slices (per 2026-06-16 slice-1 carry) — the designer happily lets an operator type any FREE ref today; slices 3–5 MUST resolve them or the "real contract" weakens at the FREE edge.

## 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS ENGINE SLICE 3a (office data-entry backend) — uncommitted

**Files:** `db/v2/migrations/0061_case_data_entries.sql`; `packages/sdk/src/caseDataEntries.ts`(+test); `apps/api/src/modules/caseDataEntries/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts`(+__tests__); guard edit `modules/reportLayouts/repository.ts:198-208`; perm `packages/access/src/permissions.ts:51,99,121,148`; wiring `http/app.ts:98`.

**VERDICT: PASS (with one SHOULD).**

### Scope discipline (Karpathy) — clean
- Backend-only; FE form correctly deferred to 3b. No speculative endpoints — exactly GET+PUT `/data-entry/tasks/:taskId`. Module mirrors platform idioms (controller→service→repository, scope-guard in repo, OCC via shared `requireVersion`, structured AppError). Every changed line traces to the slice. ✓

### Owner decisions honored — verified
- **Per-task grain.** `uq_case_data_entries_task UNIQUE (task_id)` (0061:21); one record/task. ✓
- **Dedicated office data-entry.** New perm `data_entry.manage` → MANAGER+BACKEND_USER (migration 0061:27-30) + SA via grants_all; TL/FE excluded (RBAC test → TL 403). ✓
- **Per-CPV, no default.** `findActiveByConfig` filters `client_id+product_id+kind='DATA_ENTRY' AND is_active`; partial unique idx `uq_report_layouts_active` (0060:25) ⇒ ≤1 active/CPV ⇒ `LIMIT 1` deterministic; null when unconfigured (GET 200/layout=null; save 400 NOT_CONFIGURED). No fallback/default. ✓

### Immutable-once-used guard (slice-1 carry CLOSED) — correct, one residual race
- reportLayouts.update now rejects `patch.columns` with 409 REPORT_LAYOUT_IN_USE iff `case_data_entries` has a row for the layout; rename (`name` only) still allowed (repo.ts:198-208; test "columns 409, rename OK"). Data-keyed (not kind-keyed) — correct, since only DATA_ENTRY layouts ever get keyed. idx_case_data_entries_layout backs the probe. ✓
- **SHOULD (low-sev TOCTOU):** guard's `SELECT FROM case_data_entries` runs under READ COMMITTED inside the layout's `FOR UPDATE` tx, but `repo.insert` (first-save) does NOT lock the layout row. Concurrent {re-column} vs {first-ever-save} on the same CPV ⇒ empty-check passes, re-column commits, new entry's keys orphan. **Blast radius = one task's stale optional value; self-heals (validation drops unknown keys on next save; GET renders fine). No corruption/crash/security impact.** Deterministic guard covers the common case. Hardening (deferred, not blocking dev): `FOR SHARE` on the layout row in insert, or probe inside a layout-locking tx.

### Latent-bug sweep — clean
- **PUT = full-replace** (`data = $2::jsonb`, not merge). Correct REST/idempotent semantic; 3b form MUST submit the full field set each save (omitted optional ⇒ cleared). Noted for 3b contract; not a backend bug. Test under-asserts (doesn't check prior optional cleared) — cosmetic.
- **OCC:** insert path skips `requireVersion` (first save, version omitted-OK); concurrent first-save → 23505 caught → 409 DATA_ENTRY_EXISTS. update path re-reads `before`, version-guarded UPDATE, 0 rows → `AppError.stale(before)` surfaces fresh row. requireVersion(nonnegative) ↔ SDK `version.int().min(0)` consistent. ✓
- **Validation:** required→400 DATA_ENTRY_REQUIRED (undefined|null|''); unknown keys dropped (clean[] only over layout.columns); empty-string fails required (correct). ✓
- **IDOR:** taskScope uses shared taskScopePredicate; out-of-scope/absent→null→404; non-uuid→400 (UUID_RE). Gating at route both verbs. ✓

### KNOWN CARRY (DATA_ENTRY cols reuse COMPUTED source-type) — AGREE
- Flow is source-type-agnostic (keys by column_key); works today. MANUAL source-type (catalog+CHECK+designer) is a fair follow-up. Not blocking.

**OPEN (carried):** (1) immutable-guard TOCTOU hardening (FOR SHARE on layout in insert) — low-sev, defer. (2) MANUAL source-type follow-up. (3) 3b form-contract: PUT-replace ⇒ form must submit full field set.

## 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS SLICE 3 RE-GRAIN to CASE (correction) — STAGED diff (mig 0062 staged so it shows)

**Files (12):** mig `0062_case_data_entries_case_grain.sql` (NEW, drop+recreate `uq(case_id)`); module `caseDataEntries/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts`(+api.test re-grained); SDK `caseDataEntries.ts` (`TaskDataEntry`→`CaseDataEntry`)+`client.ts`+`client.test.ts`; FE `cases/CaseDetailPage.tsx` (+187, new per-case `DataEntrySection`); `openapi.json`; `ADR-0037` Correction section.

**VERDICT: PASS (0 BLOCK, 0 must-fix FLAG, 2 low carry).**

### (1) Re-grain COMPLETE — grep-proven zero task-grain residue
Ran `grep -rn task_id|taskId|taskScope|TaskDataEntry|data-entry/tasks` over the module + sdk + apps/packages: **zero hits in the data-entry module, zero `TaskDataEntry` anywhere, zero `data-entry/tasks` anywhere.** Migration: 0061 still names `task_id` but 0062 `DROP TABLE IF EXISTS case_data_entries` + recreates `uq(case_id)` — forward-only chain, no prod v2 DB, correct (test data only). repo `taskScope`→`caseScope`, `findByTask`→`findByCase`, `TaskCpv`→`CaseCpv` (dropped now-irrelevant `status` col — was only read for the old per-task FROM, no consumer lost it). routes `/cases/:caseId`. service 404 = `CASE_NOT_FOUND`. SDK `CaseDataEntry.caseId`. FE hits `/api/v2/data-entry/cases/${caseId}`. ✓ The grain is fully CASE end-to-end.

### (2) FE perm gate MIRRORS server — exact
FE `DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE='data_entry.manage'` (CaseDetailPage:39); `canDataEntry=has(DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE)` (:74) gates the section render (:207). `has()` (:66) honors `grantsAll===true || permissions.includes(perm)` — the established JWT-perm cosmetic mirror. Server: BOTH routes `authorize(PERMISSIONS.DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE)` (routes.ts:13-14); perm → MANAGER+BACKEND_USER (permissions.ts:99,121) + SA via grants_all; api.test proves TL→403. Aligned, server authoritative. ✓

### (3) Required-validation + number/boolean coercion — correct on save (two-floor)
FE `buildData()` (CaseDetailPage): BOOLEAN → `bools[k] ?? false` (always emitted, true/false); NUMBER → `Number(v)` only after `.trim()!==''` (blank omitted, not `Number('')→0`); TEXT/DATE/SELECT → trimmed string, blank omitted. Required check `missing = required && isEmpty` disables Save + lists labels; BOOLEAN excluded from required-empty (a false checkbox is a valid answer, not "missing") — sane. Server floor re-validates against `layout.columns` (required present-or-400 `DATA_ENTRY_REQUIRED`; unknown keys dropped to `clean`). Browser-verified payload `{"property_value":7200000,"visit_done":true}` confirms number→numeric, bool→true land. ✓
- **CARRY-low (server-caught, not a bug):** FE coerces NUMBER via `Number(v)` with NO `isNaN` guard — a non-numeric typed into a `type=number` input is browser-blocked, but a pasted-then-mutated edge could send `NaN`→JSON `null`. If the column is required, server `DATA_ENTRY_REQUIRED` (null) catches it; if optional, a `null` lands. No corruption/crash. Matches slice-2 FLAG class (server-caught UX-message gap). Optional inline `isNaN` hint if the form gets polish.

### (4) OCC on re-save — correct
FE sends `version: entry.entry?.version` (undefined on first save). Service: `requireVersion(input)` called ONLY on the update branch (`existing` truthy); insert omits version (first-save legal). repo.update re-reads `before`, version-guarded UPDATE, 0 rows→`AppError.stale(before)`→409. api.test proves v99→409, v1→200→v2. FE maps `STALE_UPDATE`→"updated elsewhere — reload". ✓

### (5) Persistent case-level card UX — sane
No Cancel button (correct — it's a persistent section, not a modal). Save → `toast('Data entry saved')` + `invalidateQueries(['data-entry',caseId])` → parent `DataEntrySection` refetches → child `DataEntryFields` REMOUNTS via `key={`${caseId}:${data.entry?.version ?? 0}`}` (version bumps 1→2) → state re-initialises from freshly-saved values. Form stays open, re-hydrates, no navigation. Empty-state ("No data-entry layout configured for this case's client & product") and error/loading (HexagonLoader) branches present. Sections preserve first-appearance order; null-section columns render headingless. Browser-verified: 5 field types + sections + required markers + persist + re-hydrate + clean reload. ✓

### (6) Immutable-once-used guard — UNCHANGED, still keys off layout_id
reportLayouts/repository.ts:202 `SELECT 1 FROM case_data_entries WHERE layout_id = $1 LIMIT 1` → 409 `REPORT_LAYOUT_IN_USE`. Grain-agnostic (layout_id, not case/task_id) — the re-grain does not touch it; 0062 preserves `idx_case_data_entries_layout`. api.test "columns 409, rename OK" still passes at case grain. ✓ (The slice-3a TOCTOU OPEN — insert doesn't FOR SHARE the layout row — is UNCHANGED by this re-grain; still low-sev, still deferred.)

### Scope / frozen-standards / ADR
- **Scope-honest.** Pure re-grain — every changed line traces to task→case. `CaseCpv` correctly dropped the `status` field (dead after the task FROM left). New `caseScopePredicate` (repo.ts:23-25) is BYTE-IDENTICAL to the canonical `cases/repository.ts:186` (`created_by = ANY OR EXISTS case_tasks assigned_to = ANY`) — no forked/weaker scope logic, IDOR-safe (api.test: out-of-scope→404, non-uuid→400). Karpathy surgical: no adjacent "improvements," no creep (no generation, no v_mis_rows, no GST/invoice). ✓
- **ADR fidelity.** ADR-0037 gained a dated **Correction — 2026-06-16** section stating the per-case grain + Zion `NewDataQC` rationale (one case = one (client,product) → layout resolves cleanly per case), explicitly "Supersedes the slice-3a one-record-per-task line." Faithful to the owner's correction. ✓
- **Frozen standards.** OCC ADR-0019 intact; default-deny gating both verbs; controller→service→repo layering; UUID guard + scope-guard at both verbs. ✓

**Bottom line: PASS.** The re-grain is complete and honest — grep-proven zero task-grain residue (module/sdk/FE all `/cases/:caseId`, `CaseDataEntry`, `findByCase`/`caseScope`), the new case-scope predicate is byte-identical to the canonical cases predicate (no weaker fork, IDOR-safe), the FE `data_entry.manage` gate mirrors both server routes exactly, required-validation + number/boolean coercion are two-floor correct (FE omits-blank/emits-bool, server re-validates), OCC re-save threads `version` through the update-only branch with insert correctly version-less, the persistent card has no Cancel and re-hydrates via the `caseId:version` remount key after a toast, and the immutable-once-used guard is untouched (still keys off `layout_id`, grain-agnostic). ADR-0037 carries a dated Correction superseding the per-task line. Gate-green corroborated. No BLOCK, no must-fix FLAG.

**OPEN (carry):** (1) immutable-guard insert TOCTOU (FOR SHARE on layout row) — UNCHANGED by re-grain, low-sev, defer. (2) FE NUMBER `Number(v)` has no `isNaN` guard — server-caught, optional inline hint (slice-2 FLAG class). (3) PUT-replace contract: blanks omitted ⇒ an optional value cleared by blanking re-saves as absent — by design (full-replace), matches slice-3a carry; the per-case form submits the full field set on each save, so honored. (4) MANUAL source-type follow-up (carried).

**Files.** mig `0064_field_report_layouts.sql` (extend report_layouts: `template_body text` + `verification_type varchar(64)`, widen kind CHECK to FIELD_REPORT, coherence CHECK FIELD_REPORT⟺both-present/else-both-null, active-unique widened to `(client,product,kind,COALESCE(verification_type,''))`); new module `fieldReports/{render,repository,service,controller}.ts`(+`__tests__/{render,fieldReports.api}.test.ts`); `cases/routes.ts` (+GET `:id/tasks/:taskId/field-report`, `case.view`); `reportLayouts/{repository,service}.ts` (carry template_body/verification_type through header/list/find/insert/update; `findActiveByConfig` +optional `verificationType` 4th arg); SDK `reportLayouts.ts` (+FIELD_REPORT kind, `FieldReportView`, `refineFieldReport` superRefine, template_body/verification_type on Create/Update)+`client.ts`(+`fieldReport()`)+tests; FE `ReportLayoutsPage.tsx` (+FIELD_REPORT label, `DESIGNER_KINDS` excludes it from creatable kinds); `package.json` (+handlebars ^4.7.8); openapi(+1 path, thin-stub convention).

### Scope — CORRECT (field-only, KYC deferred per owner), zero creep
- **Field-only, KYC deferred — honored exactly.** ADR-0039 records the owner's 2026-06-16 defer-KYC decision; the build ships only the FIELD_REPORT kind + render + the per-task read. The `verification_type` free-string key (varchar(64), NOT enum-constrained) is the documented seam that lets KYC extend later with **no schema change** — present but unused, not pre-built. No KYC code, no KYC template, no KYC input surface. ✓
- **#6 card correctly left as S2 placeholder.** The diff adds the BE read endpoint + SDK method only; `CaseDetailPage` is NOT touched (the #6 `MobileReportSection` placeholder from the 2026-06-16 case-detail slice is unchanged). FE designer **excludes** FIELD_REPORT from creatable kinds (`DESIGNER_KINDS`, ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:44) — so an operator can't create a FIELD_REPORT without a template body via the column designer; rows come via API/seed until the S2 narrative designer lands. Honest deferral, matches ADR §Consequences. ✓
- **No renderer creep.** No PDF/Word/Excel, no CASE_REPORT (#9), no seeding of v1's ~180 templates — all explicitly deferred. Every changed line traces to slice-1. Karpathy-clean. ✓

### Frozen standards — all honored
- **Raw SQL only in repos.** render.ts/service.ts/controller.ts contain ZERO `query`/`pool`/SELECT; the single DB read is `fieldReportRepository.loadContext` (grep-confirmed). Layering controller→service→repository intact, mirrors caseDataEntries/cases idioms. ✓
- **Default-deny RBAC + server-side scope.** Route gates `CASE_VIEW`. `loadContext` applies `caseScopePredicate` — **byte-identical** to the canonical `cases/repository.ts` + `caseDataEntries` predicate (`cs.created_by = ANY OR EXISTS case_tasks assigned_to = ANY`), via the shared `composeScopePredicate`. Out-of-scope/absent/wrong-case → null → service throws `TASK_NOT_FOUND` 404 (IDOR-safe; api.test proves non-uuid→400, absent→404, cross-case→404). Render context (incl APPLICANT_FIELD PII) is loaded ENTIRELY under that scope predicate, so PII inherits case scope+perm (ADR §5). ✓
- **No magic numbers / no suppressions.** templateBody bounded `max(20_000)`, verificationType `max(64)` (matches DB varchar(64)). Zero eslint-disable/@ts-ignore/`any`/`as any` in the module (grep-confirmed). ✓
- **Append-only audit** n/a (read-only render path, no mutation). OCC ADR-0019 preserved on reportLayouts.update (template_body threaded through the existing version-guarded UPDATE; identity keys client/product/kind/verificationType immutable, not accepted by UpdateReportLayoutSchema — verified). ✓
- **Single-layer field result / FE≠backend result — honored.** The render context exposes `task.verification_outcome` (the FIELD/device-reported result) + `case.case_outcome` (cases.verification_outcome) and **NOT** `task_backend_reviews` (grep-confirmed none exposed). Correct: a FIELD report narrates the field exec's submitted result — it is a FE-layer surface by definition, so surfacing the FE result (not the backend official decision) is the coherent choice, not a leak. (The result-coherence concern — printing the BACKEND decision — lives on the #9 CASE_REPORT, the deferred client-facing surface; flagged there in the standing audit-series #1 risk, NOT here.) ✓

### Correctness — probed, no latent bug
- **Catalog⟺render-context coherence (the real contract).** The repo's `json_build_object` emits TASK/CASE/APPLICANT keys that **match the SOURCE_CATALOG FIXED `fields` key lists exactly** (TASK_FIELD 16 keys task_number…unit_name; CASE_FIELD 8 case_number…case_created_at; APPLICANT_FIELD 5 name/mobile/pan/applicant_type/calling_code) — verified key-by-key. So a FIXED column that passed slice-1's `validateColumnSource` allow-list resolves to a real emitted value; no silent ''→ for a valid FIXED ref. This is the slice-1 carry ("FIXED catalog must resolve to a real key") CLOSED for field reports. ✓
- **findActiveByConfig back-compat — no caller break.** New 4th arg is optional and defaults `typeClause='AND verification_type IS NULL'`; the two existing 3-arg callers (caseDataEntries 'DATA_ENTRY') still resolve correctly because DATA_ENTRY rows carry verification_type NULL (DB coherence CHECK guarantees it). service.ts:94 `byConfig` (the admin lookup) also 3-arg → matches type-less kinds. ✓
- **DB facts verified.** `verification_units.code` exists (varchar(64) NOT NULL UNIQUE UPPER_SNAKE — the stable key, matches `verification_type` width). `case_tasks.form_data` (jsonb, mig 0052), `case_tasks.applicant_id` (mig 0037), `case_tasks.verification_unit_id` (mig 0010) all present → loadContext joins are sound. Mig 0064 forward-only + idempotent (ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS / DROP-then-ADD CONSTRAINT / DROP-then-CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS), inside one BEGIN/COMMIT. ✓
- **Render security.** `Handlebars.create()` isolated instance; `compiled(data,{allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false,allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false})` blocks proto access; values HTML-escaped by HB default (render.test proves `<script>`→`&lt;script&gt;`); json-paths walked by plain property access (`walkPath`, no eval/interpolation), `null`/non-object short-circuits to undefined. `{{#eq}}` works as block AND subexpression (options-presence branch). buildContext blanks undefined/null→'' (v1 "smart placeholder" parity); cleanWhitespace collapses. ✓
- **Immutable-once-used guard UNCHANGED & correct for FIELD_REPORT.** The guard keys off `case_data_entries.layout_id` only — FIELD_REPORT persists NO keyed data (render is on-demand/stateless), so a FIELD_REPORT layout is always freely re-columnable with zero orphan risk. Correct by construction. ✓

### Gate (re-run here)
- sdk `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0; api `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0; sdk reportLayouts.test 19/19 PASS (reportLayouts.ts 100% cov); fieldReports/render.test 6/6 PASS; api+web eslint on all changed files EXIT 0; 0 suppressions in diff. The integration `fieldReports.api.test.ts` is `skipIf(!RUN)` (DB-absent in sandbox) — test code reads correct (renders narrative w/ FORM_DATA_PATH+TASK_FIELD+APPLICANT_FIELD+`{{#eq}}`; null-when-unconfigured; non-uuid 400 / absent 404 / cross-case 404).

**Bottom line: PASS.** Scope-disciplined slice-1 — field-only with KYC honestly deferred behind a zero-schema-change free-string seam, #6 card correctly still a placeholder (no FE wiring, FIELD_REPORT excluded from the column designer), renderers/CASE_REPORT/seed all deferred. Frozen standards intact: raw SQL only in the repo, scope predicate byte-identical to the canonical (IDOR-safe 404), CASE_VIEW gate, no magic numbers, no suppressions, OCC preserved, and the engine narrates the FE field result (not the backend decision) — coherent with FE≠backend. The catalog⟺render-context keys match exactly (the slice-1 FIXED-resolution carry is closed for field reports). No BLOCK, no must-fix.

**OPEN / carry (none blocking):**
1. **(observe) `narrative=null` vs error** — ADR §4 + service return null at 200 when no FIELD_REPORT configured for the vtype (parity with missing DATA_ENTRY layout). Product-correct; the S2 #6 card MUST render the null state as an honest "no report configured" empty-state (not a blank box or a JS error) — owned by the S2 card wiring.
2. **(observe, authoring) form_data keying** — slice-2 ingest stores `form_data[<formType/slug>]`; the FORM_DATA_PATH json-path is admin-authored, so the template author must use the correct top-level slug (the render test keys by unit code, which may differ from the form slug in prod). Engine is faithful (walks whatever path is configured) — this is a template-authoring caveat for the S2 designer/seed, not an engine bug. Worth a one-line note in the S2 designer help.
3. **(low, type-equality) `{{#eq}}` strictness** — `===` on values pulled from form_data (JS strings/numbers/bools) vs HB string literals: an admin comparing a numeric form value to a quoted literal (`{{#eq n "5"}}`) gets false. Acceptable for outcome-branching (outcomes are strings); document the string-compare contract when the S2 designer ships template authoring.
4. **(carry, unchanged)** the slice-1/slice-3 FREE-mode deferred-validation floor (DATA_ENTRY_FIELD/DOC_TYPE_COUNT/COMPUTED) + insert-TOCTOU on the immutable guard — untouched by this slice, still low-sev, still deferred to their consuming slices.

## 2026-06-16 — FIELD-REPORT S2a: #6 card COMBINED per-task view (raw fields + narrative, ADR-0039 R1) — uncommitted diff — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff HEAD` (4 files, +124/-11) + new `apps/api/src/modules/fieldReports/sections.ts`. Diff is purely additive on top. ✓

- **No magic numbers, no suppressions.** `SKIP_KEYS` is a named set; no `eslint-disable`/`@ts-ignore`/`any` (the `as Record<string,unknown>` casts are guarded narrowings, not suppressions). ✓
- **Raw SQL only in repos.** sections.ts is a pure helper (zero DB/SQL); service reads `ctx.formData` already loaded by the repo. ✓
- **Tokens / uppercase / `.btn-ghost` collapsible.** Outer toggle uses `className="btn-ghost"` (CaseDetailPage.tsx:1461); all colors are tokens (`text-muted-foreground`, `border-border`, `text-destructive`, `text-foreground`); section/"Generated Report" headings use `uppercase tracking-wide`. ✓

### Bugs a senior would catch — none blocking
- **Device-untrusted `form_data` — SAFE.** `buildSections` is read-only string formatting: type-guards every level (`typeof raw !== 'object' || Array.isArray` skip; nested-object values → `null` via `toValue` so no `[object Object]` leaks; arrays filtered to primitives). Output is plain text rendered by React (auto-escaped) — no injection, no crash on hostile shapes. Tests cover null/empty/system-only/nested (sections.test.ts:58-62). ✓
- **`narrative=null` + empty-sections empty-state is HONEST.** `FieldReportBody` (CaseDetailPage.tsx): when `!hasFields && narrative===null` → "No field submission yet for this task." When fields exist but no template → "No report template configured for {verificationType}." Two distinct truthful states, not a false "configure the engine" placeholder. ✓

**FLAGS (non-blocking):**
1. The accordion fires an N-fetch (one query per expanded task). Acceptable: lazy on expand, `enabled: open`, keyed cache — see Principal ledger. Not a CEO blocker.
2. **(carry)** immutable-guard insert TOCTOU + FREE-mode deferred-validation floor — untouched by this slice, still deferred.

**Bottom line: PASS.** Scope-tight (R1, photos deferred), standards-clean, empty-states honest, untrusted-blob handling safe. Gates green (pnpm verify EXIT=0; sdk 133 / api 669 incl sections.test 5; web build green; browser-verified :5273). Cleared to commit.

### Scope correctness — clean, no creep
- **Exactly the two promised surfaces.** (a) Designer: `DESIGNER_KINDS = LAYOUT_KINDS` (FIELD_REPORT no longer filtered out, ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:41-44), gated FIELD_REPORT-only verificationType select + templateBody textarea, columns relabeled "Variables". ### verificationType-immutable-on-edit — CORRECT, and defended in depth
- **It IS an identity key** (part of `uq_report_layouts_active` COALESCE index, mig 0064:34-35) — changing it would silently re-bucket a layout and could collide with another active row. Locking it on edit is the right call, and it mirrors the existing client/product/kind `disabled={isEdit}` convention (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:264,280,297 vs the new 322). ✓
- **Three independent locks, not one.** (1) FE disables the select on edit; (2) FE save only sends `verificationType` on CREATE (`...(isFieldReport ? { verificationType, templateBody } : {})` in the POST branch; PUT branch sends only `templateBody`); (3) `UpdateReportLayoutSchema` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:274-282) does NOT even accept `verificationType` — a rogue PUT carrying it is rejected by zod, never reaches SQL. Belt + braces + server-authoritative. ✓

### Frozen standards — pass
- **No phantom classes.** Uses `.input`, `.btn`, `.btn-ghost` — all defined in index.css:8-14. No `.btn-primary`. ✓
- **Focus-trap dialog untouched & intact** — `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal` + `aria-label` + `dialogRef` all pre-existing (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:246-251); this slice adds fields INSIDE the trapped container, doesn't alter the trap. ✓
- **No magic numbers / no suppressions** — `fieldUnits` filter is `kind === 'FIELD_VISIT'` (the SDK enum value, not a literal); textarea `min-h-[8rem]` is a tailwind utility (token-scale), not a hard pixel; placeholder strings are help text. No `any`/ts-ignore/eslint-disable in the diff. ✓
- **Tokens only** — `text-foreground`, `text-muted-foreground`, `font-mono` etc.; the `text-[11px]` helper-caption size matches the existing small-print idiom on the page. ✓

### Bugs a senior would catch — none blocking
- **Hydration once, both new fields.** The `if (isEdit && detail.data && !hydrated)` block sets `verificationType`/`templateBody` from `d` alongside the existing fields (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:136-137) and the `!hydrated` guard fires exactly once — no re-hydration churn. `d.verificationType ?? ''` / `d.templateBody ?? ''` correctly coerce the nullable contract to controlled-input strings. ✓
- **canSave gate is correct on BOTH modes.** `(!isFieldReport || (templateBody.trim() !== '' && (isEdit || verificationType !== '')))` — non-FIELD_REPORT unaffected; FIELD_REPORT create requires BOTH body+type; FIELD_REPORT edit requires only body (type is locked/absent). Matches the create/update schema requirements exactly (Create needs both, Update needs only mutable body). ✓
- **Type-less callers unbroken.** by-config without the param → service passes `undefined` → repo `AND verification_type IS NULL` → DATA_ENTRY/MIS/BILLING_MIS resolve exactly as before. The new api test asserts this (FIELD_REPORT-without-type → null at 200). ✓
- **No `[object Object]` / empty-string poisoning.** Service trims and coerces (`vt.trim() ? vt.trim() : undefined`); empty/whitespace param degrades to the type-less path (not an empty-string match the `verification_type <> ''` CHECK forbids). ✓

### Gate (authoritative, per kickoff)
`pnpm verify` EXIT=0 — sdk 133, api 670 (+1 byConfig test), web build, **openapi UNCHANGED** (by-config reads loose `rawQuery`, not a strict schema, so a new optional query param doesn't move the contract — consistent), no flake. (2) The dependency direction is already correct and one-way (fieldReports → reportLayouts; no cycle), and importing a sibling DOMAIN's read method is a legitimate domain-to-domain reference, not a boundary violation. (3) The project's own precedent is module-local copy over premature sharing (caseScopePredicate, now 5 copies) — `findActiveByConfig` is the OPPOSITE case (a single canonical READ everyone should share, NOT duplicate), so the right outcome is "keep the shared import," not "fork it" and not "hoist it to infra." The ratchet was a tripwire to FORCE this decision, not a mandate to promote; the decision has now been made deliberately and documented. **Ratchet CLOSED.** The previous standing carry "(1) promote findActiveByConfig" is RETIRED.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** Scope-tight (designer + by-config only), identity-key immutability correct and triply-enforced, frozen standards clean, hydration once, gates green + browser-verified. No BLOCK, no must-fix. Ratchet ruled CLOSED (keep+document, don't promote).

## 2026-06-16 — FIELD-REPORT S3a: grammar-helper library + plain-text (noEscape) render + envelope skip-keys (ADR-0039) — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff HEAD` (4 files) + NEW `fieldReports/helpers.ts`. CEO lens: scope, v1 fidelity, the noEscape decision, standards.

### Scope — TIGHT, no creep
Exactly the three things the slice promised: (a) a helper LIBRARY (helpers.ts — ~30 grammar helpers ported from v1, plus the `eq` block helper relocated here, plus the exported shared `hb` instance); (b) the render switched to PLAIN TEXT (`render.ts` one-line `noEscape: true` + the import move); (c) SKIP_KEYS extended with v1 envelope keys (`sections.ts`). The two test-file edits are consequences (render.test escape→plain-text flip; api-test column rename to dodge the helper-name collision). Nothing speculative — no new endpoint, no schema change, no PDF/Word work (correctly left to S5), no KYC (carved out per ADR). ✓

### v1 fidelity — the grammar MATCHES prod
This is the load-bearing CEO concern (the narrative is what the bank sees). Spot-checked ordinal/pluralize/nameplate/callRemark/documentShown plus the rest against `CRM-BACKEND/TemplateReportService.ts` — every helper is a line-for-line port of its v1 original, same literal output strings, same edge-case branches (Bug-125 free-text doc recognition, Bug-135 never-UTC date, Bug-133 APF verdict coherence, the `|| 'N/A'` nameplate fallback). Live :4000 + :5273 confirmed it end-to-end: a helper-rich template rendered `...Door nameplate shows the name "MAYUR". RAJESH is salaried. Door was open.` — pluralize/nameplate(literal quotes)/lc/eq all correct, #6 card shows literal quotes with NO HTML entities, 0 console errors. The prose the operator sees is byte-faithful to v1. ✓

### The noEscape decision — CORRECT
The narrative is genuinely PLAIN TEXT: v1 prints literal quotes (`shows the name "X"`), and HTML-encoding would corrupt the prose into `&quot;`/`&lt;` inside what is a text document, not an HTML fragment. So the engine MUST NOT entity-encode — `noEscape: true` is right. Output-encoding is correctly DELEGATED to the consumer: the #6 card renders the string as a React text node (auto-escaped by React → XSS-safe), and the comment on render.ts:71-73 explicitly puts the encoding obligation on S5's PDF/Word/HTML renderers. This is the correct security boundary for a multi-target render: encode at the OUTPUT sink (per context), not at the prose-generation source. The defence-in-depth proto-flags (allowProto*ByDefault:false) are RETAINED — noEscape does not loosen them. ✓

### Standards — clean
No magic numbers (SKIP_KEYS are domain envelope strings, documented + lowercase to match the existing lookup; the regexes are the v1 grammar contracts). No suppressions — zero `any`/ts-ignore/eslint-disable in the diff. `str()` (helpers.ts:15) is a deliberate, documented coercion (the object→'' rule is what makes optional helper args safe), not a sloppy cast. Templates remain admin-authored (SUPER_ADMIN, report_template.manage). ✓

### COLLISION RULING (CEO concurrence)
A column `columnKey` equal to a helper name (e.g. `area`) is SHADOWED by the helper — the api-test hit it and the CTO fixed it by renaming the column to `loc` + an NB comment. **CEO CONCURS with the CTO: documenting the collision rule now + deferring a HARD designer-side guard to S3b is ACCEPTABLE; do NOT block S3a on it.** Rationale I accept: (1) it is not silent — a shadowed key renders visibly-wrong/empty prose in the #6 preview the author is already looking at, so it surfaces at authoring time, not in front of the bank; (2) it is not a data-integrity or security path; (3) the guard's natural home is the DESIGNER (the S3b authoring-UX slice that already owns the `{{#eq}}` numeric note + the FORM_DATA_PATH slug caveat), and the reserved-name set is now exportable from helpers.ts for that validator; (4) bolting a backend reject onto S3a would be scope-creep into S3b's lane. The rule is documented in BOTH ledgers so it cannot be lost. **Collision = KNOWN, deferred to S3b. Not a must-fix.**

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** Scope-tight (helper lib + plain-text + skip-keys, nothing more), v1 grammar faithful (spot-checks line-for-line + live-rendered byte-correct), noEscape is the right call (plain-text prose, consumer output-encodes, proto-guards retained), standards clean. Collision ruled KNOWN+deferred-to-S3b. No BLOCK, no must-fix.

GATE NOTE: the slice's own surface is fully green — fieldReports 26/26 + 3 RUN-gated skip = 29 (helpers 14 + render 7 + sections 5 + integration 3). The full `pnpm verify` did not show EXIT=0 in this review's shell, but the failures are pure local ENV/infra (a missing-`DATABASE_URL` cascade on the first run → 11 fails; with `.env` sourced → api 681/684, the 3 residual being local-fixture gaps: locations pincode-sort seed, system health payload shape, users profile-photo 503 STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED with no object store provisioned). None touch fieldReports — consistent with the kickoff's authoritative "684 + documented rotating auth-lockout flake."

OPEN/carry (none blocking, all S3b/S5/ADR-deferred): (2) `{{#eq}}` numeric-vs-string designer note; (3) FORM_DATA_PATH slug-match authoring caveat; (4) PDF/Word + KYC field-reports deferred; (5) NEW — helper/columnKey name-collision designer guard deferred to S3b (export reserved-name set from helpers.ts).

## 2026-06-17 — FIELD_PHOTO reverse-geocode: S4 foundation (mig 0065 + ADR-0040) + Slice A (resolver + on-view write-through + #7 caption + SDK) — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff bb0e1d1` (11 files: openapi, cases controller/repository/routes/service, cases.api.test, web CaseDetailPage, mig 0065 [real path `db/v2/migrations/`, the diff-stat `apps/api/migrations/` is cosmetic], ADR-0040, sdk cases.ts/client.ts) + cross-checked geocode service/seam + insertFieldAttachment kind. CEO lens: scope discipline (attachment≠photo), evidence integrity, degradation, standards, the slice cut.

### Scope discipline — the owner's attachment(OFFICE_REF) ≠ photo(FIELD_PHOTO) rule HOLDS, everywhere
This was the load-bearing check and it passes cleanly. Reverse-geocode is FIELD_PHOTO-only at every touchpoint:
- **Resolve read** `fieldPhotoForGeocode` (repository.ts:1431) — `WHERE … ca.kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO'`. An OFFICE_REF id → 0 rows → service throws `FIELD_PHOTO_NOT_FOUND` (service.ts:454) → 404. ✓
- **Write-through** `setFieldPhotoReverseGeocodedAddress` (repository.ts:1442) — `WHERE … kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO' AND reverse_geocoded_address IS NULL`. Can never stamp an address onto an OFFICE_REF row. ✓
- **#7 list** `listFieldPhotos` (repository.ts:1366) already FIELD_PHOTO-filtered; the new SELECT only ADDS the `reverse_geocoded_address` column — no kind change. ✓
- **Office octet-stream path UNTOUCHED.** Diff contains ZERO code lines referencing OFFICE_REF (the 3 hits are comment/ADR prose documenting the exclusion). `uploadAttachment` / `insertAttachment` (kind='OFFICE_REF', ADR-0025 backend→mobile download) are not in the diff. No geocode enqueue on the office path. ✓
The shared-table mig-0055 pattern is honest: the geo-CHECK + freeze trigger sit on `case_attachments` and are INERT for OFFICE_REF (geo NULL → CHECK passes; address never set → `OLD.reverse_geocoded_address IS NOT NULL` guard never fires). Behavior is photo-only **by rule**, schema is shared **by table** — matches the ADR's explicit framing.

### Product correctness — evidence integrity is real, degradation is correct
- **Frozen server value, device never geocodes.** Address is the server's `reverse_geocoded_address` (server Google key per ADR-0040/ADR-0026); the device sends raw `{lat,lng,accuracy,timestamp}` only. FE renders `photo.reverseGeocodedAddress ?? addr?.address` — always a server value, never a device-computed one. ✓
- **Freeze is DB-level, not app-level** (mig 0065:33-50) — a BEFORE-UPDATE trigger permits exactly NULL→address; any address→different or address→NULL `RAISE EXCEPTION`. Tamper-evident at the row, not just the code path. The write-through is freeze-SAFE by construction: NULL-guarded UPDATE means a concurrent already-set row matches 0 rows, then the re-SELECT returns the pre-existing frozen value — the trigger is never even reached on the race. Test "second view is cached / a later differing geocoder must NOT change the frozen value" proves the early-return + freeze jointly (cases.api.test.ts:2200-2214). ✓
- **On-view fallback resolves+persists** (service.ts resolveFieldPhotoAddress): address set → `{cached:true}` no geocoder call; no coords → `{address:null,cached:false}` no geocoder call (test GEO3 asserts `called===false`); else cache-first `geocodeService.reverse` → persist → return frozen. Idempotent + write-through-safe exactly as the ADR decision #3 states. ✓
- **Graceful degradation.** Google miss / no key → `geocodeService.reverse` returns `address:null` (NOT cached, self-heals once keyed) → service returns `{address:null}` → FE shows raw coords `lat.toFixed(6), lng.toFixed(6) (±Nm)` + a Maps link, and capture-time. No page break, no upload coupling (geocode is a separate GET). The `enabled: !reverseGeocodedAddress && hasCoords` query gate means a no-coords photo never even fires the resolve. ✓

### Standards — clean
- **No XSS.** Every surfaced value is a React text node: `{address}` (title attr too), coords via numeric `.toFixed`, accuracy via `Math.round`, time via `new Date(...).toLocaleString()`. `mapsHref` is interpolated from lat/lng guarded by `hasCoords` (`typeof === 'number'`) — no string injection into the href. Address is a server-trusted Google `formatted_address`; even so React auto-escapes it. ✓
- **Conventions.** `.btn`/token classes preserved; the thumb refactor splits the old single `<a>`-wrapper into an image `<a>` + a metadata block inside the SAME `rounded-md border border-border` card (necessary — a Maps `<a>` can't nest inside the image `<a>`; valid-HTML fix, not gratuitous). `text-muted-foreground`/`text-primary`/`line-clamp-2` are existing tokens. unitName now conditionally rendered (was an empty `''` div) — minor tidy within the touched component, acceptable. ✓
- **No magic numbers / suppressions.** `toFixed(6)` matches the cache's documented 6-dp grid (geocode service COORD_DECIMALS=6); DLQ `numeric(10,7)/(11,7)` are standard lat/lng precision; no `any`/ts-ignore/eslint-disable in the diff. The `lat!`/`lng!` non-null asserts are guarded by `hasCoords`. openapi correctly registers the new GET (loose phase-2 response stub, consistent with sibling routes — no contract drift). ✓

### The slice cut — Foundation + Slice A together is the RIGHT minimal vertical
Foundation (mig 0065 freeze/CHECK/DLQ + ADR) is valid standalone (schema-level guarantees don't need the app layer). Slice A delivers the user-visible feature with the on-view write-through as its own recovery net — which is precisely why deferring Slice B (async-on-upload queue/worker/DLQ-insert/replay) is SAFE: the on-view fallback already backfills any row, so B is a pure-performance pre-warm + reliability layer, not a correctness prerequisite. Slice C (#9 CASE_REPORT photo context) correctly lands with S5's report work. The `reverse_geocode_dlq` table ships in foundation but is currently WRITTEN BY NOBODY (no insert until Slice B) — acceptable as a forward-declared schema artifact, flagged below so it isn't mistaken for live. The cut is disciplined: no queue, no worker, no report-ctx, no KYC in this diff.

### Gate
CTO gate accepted GREEN modulo the documented rotating flake (reportTemplates 33/33 isolated; cases field-photo 4/4 — the 4 new ADR-0040 tests: resolve+freeze+cached, null-result, no-coords-no-call, unknown-id 404/IDOR-safe). LIVE Google E2E (resolve→persist→frozen→cached) + browser caption verified 0 console errors. The 404 test confirms the scope-guard is IDOR-safe (unknown attachmentId under a valid case → 404, no leak). Contracts cross-verified independently: `ReverseGeocodeResult {address,cached}` (sdk/geocode.ts:6), `geocodeService.reverse` cache-first wrapper, `setGeocoder` test seam all exist as the diff assumes.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit + push.** Scope-tight (FIELD_PHOTO-only at resolver/repo/write-through/caption; office octet-stream path zero-touch), evidence integrity is DB-enforced (freeze trigger) not just app-level, degradation to coords+Maps is correct, on-view fallback is idempotent+freeze-safe, standards clean (no XSS, tokens, no magic/suppressions), and Foundation+Slice-A is the correct minimal cut with B/C rightly deferred. No BLOCK, no must-fix.

**OPEN / carry (none blocking):**
1. **(Slice B)** `reverse_geocode_dlq` ships in mig 0065 but has ZERO writers until Slice B's worker (DLQ insert on retry-exhaustion + admin replay). Forward-declared schema — confirm Slice B wires the insert + a replay surface, else the table is permanently dead. Async-on-upload enqueue must ALSO be FIELD_PHOTO-only (re-assert the scope rule in B; the office upload path must NOT enqueue).
2. **(Slice C)** `reverseGeocodedAddress` into the #9 CASE_REPORT photo context — lands with S5; the SDK/repo field is already in place to feed it.
3. **(mobile re-assert)** ADR-0040's "device MUST NOT geocode (server-only key)" invariant must be re-checked on any mobile change — mobile is a SEPARATE repo; nothing in this diff enforces it on the device side.
4. **(observe)** the freeze trigger is table-wide BEFORE-UPDATE on `case_attachments` — inert for OFFICE_REF today, but any future column that legitimately needs to clear/rewrite `reverse_geocoded_address` (e.g. a deliberate admin re-geocode) would have to go THROUGH a trigger change, by design. Correct now; note it so a future "let admin re-resolve" feature doesn't silently fight the trigger.

VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit). 2 FLAGs + 2 NITs, all NON-BLOCKING.**
  - **Frozen invariants — pass.** (a) **Narrative+sections plain text** per ADR §3 — service passes `fr.narrative`/`fr.sections` straight through into JSON; encoding is the renderer's job, correctly deferred to slices 2/4/5 (service.ts:76-77). (b) **attachment≠photo** — `WHERE ca.kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO'` (repository.ts:40). (c) **Single-layer result** — reads `detail.verificationOutcome` (case) + `t.verificationOutcome` (task) only; no `task_backend_reviews`, no FE-only field; v1 fragmentation structurally absent (service.ts:72,139). (d) **Default-deny + scope-404** — `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` + `caseRepository.findById(caseId, scope)` returns null → 404 (routes.ts:63, service.ts:29-30); same scope contract as `GET /cases/:id`. (e) **No magic numbers** — `MS_PER_DAY=86_400_000`, `UUID_RE`, page constants from SDK `REPORT_PAGE_SIZES/_ORIENTATIONS`. No `any`/ts-ignore/eslint-disable in diff. (f) **OCC + migration** — 0066 is forward-only + idempotent (`ALTER … IF NOT EXISTS`, `DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS`); kind CHECK widened; CASE_REPORT coherence CHECK requires `(template_body + page_size ∈ {A4,LETTER,LEGAL} + page_orientation ∈ {portrait,landscape} + verification_type IS NULL)`; the unique `uq_report_layouts_active … COALESCE(verification_type,'')` already enforces one active CASE_REPORT per (client, product).
  - **Scope discipline (Karpathy) — clean.** Every changed line traces to S5/1. SDK adds `caseReports.ts` (typed context contract), `reportLayouts.ts` widens LAYOUT_KINDS + adds REPORT_PAGE_SIZES/_ORIENTATIONS + pageSize/pageOrientation on ReportLayout; client gets `cases.reportPreview`. No adjacent "improvements," no speculative abstraction.
  - **FLAG-1 (NON-BLOCKING, coherence) — scope-asymmetry between tasks-array and photos-totals.** `caseRepository.findById` uses `caseScopePredicate` and returns ALL tasks once the case is visible (cases/repository.ts:495-509); `caseReportRepository.listPhotosForReport` uses `taskScopePredicate` (caseReports/repository.ts:25-34). For an actor whose case-grain visibility exceeds their task-grain visibility (FIELD_AGENT chiefly: case visible via one assigned task, but task-scope caps photos to their own task), `totals.photoCount = photoRows.length` is task-scoped while per-task `photos: []` arrays for tasks they're NOT on are silently empty (service.ts:78,90). Totals can therefore disagree with the sum of per-task photo arrays. Pre-existing case-vs-task asymmetry inherited from `GET /cases/:id`; not introduced here. **DISPOSITION:** NON-BLOCKING for Slice 1 (JSON only, FE/Designer consumption). MUST be reconciled in Slice 3 BEFORE the PDF renderer ships — a client report whose totals don't reconcile to its body is the v1 result-fragmentation pattern in a new guise. Carry-forward: either (i) gate the endpoint to roles whose case-scope ≡ task-scope (BACKEND_USER/MANAGER/SA), or (ii) recompute totals from the displayed task array (consistency from the same source), or (iii) widen photos to case-scope when the case itself is in scope (since the case already showed all task narratives, the photos shown on the same page are not a new disclosure).
  - **FLAG-2 (NON-BLOCKING, test gap) — no negative-perm / no out-of-scope-404 in slice's own suite.** `caseReports.api.test.ts:280-286` covers happy-path + layout-pointer + 400(not-a-uuid) + 404(unknown-uuid) under SUPER_ADMIN. Missing: role-without-`case.view` → 403, and MANAGER on a case outside hierarchy → 404 (the IDOR-safe path). The default-deny + scope-404 invariants are PROVEN via the shared `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` + `caseScopePredicate` (independently tested in `cases.api.test.ts`), so the gates work at runtime — but the slice's own suite doesn't lock them in. **DISPOSITION:** NON-BLOCKING (gate is shared infra, not novel here). Tighten alongside the Slice-3 PDF renderer tests, where the same endpoint shape gains output-encoding assertions.
  - **NIT-1 — `userName` returns 'Unknown' for a deleted/missing actor row** (service.ts:122). Acceptable degraded fallback; ADR is silent. Will surface only in pathological "deleted-user generates report" cases.
  - **NIT-2 — per-task FIELD_REPORT render in `Promise.all` re-resolves scope and re-reads the case per task** (service.ts:33-35). ADR §"Negative" already calls this out as acceptable given report-generation is low-frequency. Revisit if hot in Slice 3 load-test.
  - **Gate evidence (per the brief):** `pnpm verify` green modulo documented rotating load-flake (cases.api Parse Error this run; 66/66 in isolation). SDK 160/160. Live HTTP E2E on dev :4000 against CASE-000030: 200 + correct assembly; 400 on `not-a-uuid`; 404 on unknown UUID; 401 unauth. Live evidence + isolation matches the suite contract. Accepted.
  - **OPEN (carry forward into Slice 3 / Designer):** (1) reconcile FLAG-1 scope asymmetry BEFORE the PDF renderer goes user-visible; (2) add negative-perm + out-of-scope-404 tests in slice's own suite; (3) the `{{{raw}}}` lint gate (ADR §2/§7) — not in scope here (no template authoring yet) but is a hard BLOCK-level invariant for Slice 2 (Designer save) and Slice 3 (renderer compile); (4) audit-log row insert into `case_reports_generated` (ADR §8) — deferred to Slice 3, not in Slice 1.

(The inline `#111/#ccc/#f3f3f3` hex live INSIDE `DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE` — correct: that is a self-contained print document Puppeteer will rasterize, NOT app chrome; it must be asset-free inline CSS, design tokens don't apply to a print sheet.) Blob-URL `window.open(..., 'noopener')` + 60s revoke is the right pattern for an auth-bearing (Bearer header) document a plain `<a href>` can't carry.
- **Bugs/risks — none blocking.** Helpers `badge`/`eq` are registered AFTER `DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE` is declared but registration runs at module-load before any `compile()` call → fine (NIT only: reads slightly out of order). `fmtDate` ISO-slice is TZ-stable by design. `setTimeout(revoke, 60s)` leaks the object URL if the tab is closed early — bounded, negligible. No XSS, no IDOR, no scope widening, no contract drift (no openapi change — `.html` returns `text/html`, not a JSON contract).

**Gate:** `render.test.ts` **5/5 PASS** (coverage-disabled run; the single-file 85% global-coverage ERROR is the suite-wide threshold, not a test failure). The 2 new `caseReports.api.test.ts` live cases (html renders + escapes `<script>` applicant name; 400 bad-uuid / 404 unknown) are `RUN`-gated (live DB) — accept under the CTO live gate, consistent with Slice 1's suite posture.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit + push.** Scope-tight (HTML render only; Puppeteer/docx/xlsx/audit-table deferred), the plain-text-narrative SINK output-encodes (auto-escape ON, no `{{{`, nl2br escape-first, proto blocked, img-attr-breakout safe), the default template is a credible bank report showing the OFFICIAL result + dates with all field names schema-valid, UX is tokens-only on-system, and FLAG-1 is carried-not-regressed. No BLOCK, no must-fix.

**OPEN / carry (none blocking):**
1. **(FLAG-1, → Slice 3 BEFORE PDF goes user-visible)** task-scoped photos vs case-scoped tasks → `totals.photoCount` can disagree with the sum of per-task photo arrays for an actor whose case-grain visibility > task-grain (FIELD_AGENT). Now ALSO surfaced in the rendered HTML, not just JSON. Reconcile (gate to case≡task-scope roles, OR recompute totals from the displayed array, OR widen photos to case-scope) before the PDF download ships.
2. **(Slice 2/3)** `{{{`-reject lint gate at Designer save (ADR §2/§7) — the render engine here REFUSES nothing on the input body (it just auto-escapes `{{var}}`); a future admin body using `{{{` WOULD bypass escaping. The renderer is safe for the built-in default + `{{}}` bodies; the BLOCK-level lint gate must land at Slice 2/3 save before any admin-authored body is persisted.
3. **(Slice 3)** audit-log insert into `case_reports_generated` (ADR §8) — still deferred; lands with the PDF download (the artifact worth auditing).
4. **(Slice 1 carry, still open)** negative-perm 403 + out-of-scope-404 in the slice's OWN suite — the `.html` route reuses the same `authorize(CASE_VIEW)`+scope-guard (the new 404 test exercises scope; a `role-without-view`→403 case is still not locked in the suite).

## 2026-06-17 — S5 Slice 2b CASE_REPORT PDF as a background job + PDF button (ADR-0041) — VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit). 0 BLOCK. **CEO FLAG-1 → RESOLVED.**

**Diff reviewed (`git diff HEAD`, all tracked):** NEW `platform/pdf/index.ts` (lazy-singleton Puppeteer + FIFO concurrency gate + setContent/pdf timeouts) + `pdf.test.ts`; NEW `modules/caseReports/job.ts` (`CaseReportJobProcessor`). - **🎯 FLAG-1 — RESOLVED (option iii, the right one).** `listPhotosForReport(caseId)` dropped the `taskScopePredicate` leg and is now **CASE-scoped** — it returns ALL of the case's `FIELD_PHOTO` rows once the caller has proven case visibility (`assemble`→`caseRepository.findById(caseId,scope)`; `enqueueReport`→`caseRepository.caseVisible(caseId,scope)`, both via the identical `caseScopePredicate`). The long justification comment is **correct**: `findById` already returns ALL tasks of a visible case (tasks aren't individually scoped), so the old per-task photo predicate was *stricter than task visibility* — a colleague's task on a case I can see rendered 0 photos while still counting in `totals.photoCount`. Now photos and tasks draw from the **same case-scoped row set**, so the math invariant `Σ(task.photos.length) === totals.photoCount` holds (the orphan-`task_id` filter is retained, applied to both sides). **Product view: a user who can see a case now sees ALL its field photos in the report — no NEW disclosure** (the case page already showed every task's narrative under the same gate; the photos sit on the same page). The 2a auditor's "report whose totals don't reconcile to its body = v1 fragmentation reborn" is closed before the PDF ships user-visible. Karpathy-clean: every line traces to 2b.
- **Frozen invariants — hold.** (a) Result single-layer: PDF renders the SAME `assemble()` HTML, reading only `case.verificationOutcome`/`task.outcome`; no `task_backend_reviews`, no FE field, no new result column. Security's 2a finding carries unchanged. (c) attachment≠photo: `WHERE kind='FIELD_PHOTO'` retained.
- **The async choice — honoured cleanly, no half-measure.** Owner chose async over sync: `POST /:id/report` → **202 + PENDING JobView**, worker re-resolves the SAME scope from the payload actor, renders, stores at `case-reports/${actor.userId}/${jobId}.pdf`, returns `{storageKey,filename,caseId}`; FE invalidates `JOBS_KEY` + toasts "will appear in the tray"; tray shows progress (15/45/70/90); download via the **shared** `GET /jobs/:id/result-url` presigned path (own-job-scoped `getOwned`, double-locked by the userId-namespaced key). The bell DOWNLOAD action generalised `type==='EXPORT'`→`DOWNLOAD_TYPES` set. This reuses the EXPORT job pattern wholesale — no bespoke queue. Access gated at enqueue (immediate scope-404 IDOR-safe, not a FAILED job) AND re-gated in the worker. Sound product UX for a bank operator and the right call (Puppeteer is heavy; blocking a request thread up to 90s would be worse).
- **Product sense / client-facing quality — credible.** Real-Puppeteer test (`pdf.test.ts` 2/2 PASS, ~31s) produces a valid `%PDF-` buffer, honours A4/LETTER + landscape, reuses the browser, handles `disconnected` (drops the cached promise → relaunch) and always closes the page in `finally`. Container-safe flags (`--no-sandbox` justified: input is our own trusted HTML). Print margins set. The official `verificationOutcome` prints as Case Result. Good.
- **Bugs/risks — none blocking.** Concurrency gate traced correct (release does `active--` then resolves a waiter that does `active++`: net-neutral, waiter holds the slot). Singleton-launch promise-cached + cleared on failure/disconnect. Live E2E test proves enqueue→`awaitAllJobs`→SUCCEEDED→presigned-url 200 + 400/404 IDOR. Mig 0067 forward-only/idempotent (`DROP … IF EXISTS` + re-add CHECK). NIT: Chromium adds ~280MB to the API/worker image (ADR-acknowledged); cold first-render ~1-2s — acceptable for a low-freq action.

No BLOCK, no must-fix.

NO `exceljs`, NO Designer touch, NO new migration/route shape. `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS=['pdf','docx']` — **xlsx is deliberately ABSENT**, so a `?format=xlsx` request 400s (`BAD_REQUEST{param:format}`) and the Excel button stays `disabled title="Coming soon"`. No creep. Every line traces to Slice 4.
- **Product sense — a CREDIBLE editable client deliverable.** Built PROGRAMMATICALLY from the typed `CaseReportContext` (not an HTML/image dump): H1 client + subtitle + caseNumber·status header; Case key/value grid-table; Applicants table; per-task H3 heading + italic subject line + plain-text narrative (one Paragraph per line, line-breaks preserved) + per-section grid-tables + `ImageRun`-embedded photos with a GPS/geocode/date caption; footer with generated-by + the positive/negative/refer/fraud + photo totals. This is genuinely editable Word — an ops user CAN tweak it before sending (a real win over the sealed PDF). Image fetch degrades to caption-only on any failure (15s timeout, never fails the whole report). Good.
- **Result-coherence — HELD.** Prints the OFFICIAL result: `case.verificationOutcome` ("Case Result" row, docx.ts:185) + per-task `task.outcome` (heading `[outcome]`), both sourced from the single-layer `verification_outcome` columns the assembly engine reads (service.ts:117,184). Same `CaseReportContext` as HTML/PDF — ONE assembly, three sinks. No new result column. ✓
- **Output-encoding — structural, safe.** Every value goes through `docx` `TextRun`, which serializes a plain-text run (OOXML XML-encodes; no markup parse). docx.test.ts:81-93 proves `<script>alert(1)</script>` in customerName never appears as live markup in the zip. Security owns the depth review; structurally there is no injection sink here. ✓
- **attachment≠photo — HELD.** Only `task.photos` (FIELD_PHOTO, assembled upstream) are embedded; zero OFFICE_REF path in the renderer. ✓
- **Worker wiring — correct.** ONE JobType (CASE_REPORT) parameterized by format; docx MIME = `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document`; storageKey `case-reports/${userId}/${jobId}.docx`; actor re-resolves the SAME scope on the worker → report contains only what the user may see. Shared tray + presigned download.

## 2026-06-17 — S5 Slice 5 (FINAL) CASE_REPORT Excel (.xlsx) renderer + Excel button (ADR-0041) — VERDICT: PASS (clear to commit). 0 BLOCK. **xlsx carry → RESOLVED. S5 COMPLETE.**
- **Carry closure + scope — TIGHT (Karpathy-clean).** The xlsx carry (Slice 5, the LAST CASE_REPORT format) is RESOLVED. Diff is EXACTLY the exceljs renderer + the minimal wiring to reach it: NEW `xlsx.ts`, +1 MIME entry + 1 ternary arm in `job.ts`, `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS += 'xlsx'` (sdk), FE Excel button un-disabled + mutation type widened to `CaseReportFormat`, +2 tests. NO Designer touch, NO new migration/route, NO new JobType. Every line traces to Slice 5. No creep.
- **Product — a 3-sheet workbook IS a credible bank-ops Excel deliverable.** The split is the RIGHT product decision: narrative documents (the rendered case story, photos, branding) → PDF/Word; structured DATA → Excel. The 3 sheets serve real ops needs: (1) Case Summary = the case at-a-glance (identity/result/TAT/totals); (2) Per-Task Outcomes = one row/task, sortable+filterable by outcome/verification/date — a reviewer can pivot/AutoFilter across a batch; (3) Photo Manifest = one row/photo with GPS lat/lng/accuracy/frozen-address/capture-time + the presigned URL — an auditable evidence index. Numeric cells (lat/lng/accuracy/photo-count) are written as NUMBERS not text, so sort/filter/pivot actually work (Principal confirmed not csvSafe-stringified). Photos are LISTED not embedded (file-bloat/cell-size) — correct for a data export. This is what a bank ops analyst reconciling 100 verifications/day reaches for; the PDF/Word is what they forward to the client. Credible.
- **Result-coherence — HELD.** Case Summary prints `ctx.case.verificationOutcome` (the OFFICIAL result, xlsx.ts:52) — same source the PDF/Word/HTML sinks use; no FE/stale leak into the client-facing Excel.
- **Security — formula-injection guarded.** Every free-text cell flows through `csvSafe` (prefix `'` on `=/+/-/@/tab/CR`) so a malicious applicant name/narrative can't become a live formula in Excel/Sheets. URLs are emitted as PLAIN TEXT not HYPERLINK() formulas (the ADR spec'd hyperlinks; the build chose text to keep the injection surface closed) — a security-superior deviation, documented. Unit-tested (3/3).
- **ADR closure — "one assembly engine, three sinks (+HTML preview)" fully realized.** S5 is now COMPLETE: HTML preview (slice 2a) + PDF (2b, Puppeteer) + Word (4, docx) + Excel (5, exceljs), all from ONE `CaseReportContext` via ONE `CASE_REPORT` JobType parameterized by `format`, ONE job tray, ONE presigned-download path. This is the lever that replaces v1's ~180 hardcoded templates + one-off PDF service with a config-driven multi-format engine — the Zion-equivalent downloadable report. Worth noting as a milestone: the CASE_REPORT template-report engine epic is DONE.
- **OPEN (carried):** (1) **DPDP** — stored artifacts at `case-reports/${userId}/${jobId}.{pdf,docx,xlsx}` (PII: customer name/phone/PAN + geotagged photos + GPS in the manifest) STILL have NO TTL/lifecycle sweep; xlsx adds a THIRD stored-artifact format to the same retention gap. The Photo Manifest sheet makes GPS/address machine-extractable, modestly raising the minimisation stakes. Add retention before scale. *(still OPEN)* (2) **Worker observability** — no dedicated metric/alert on CASE_REPORT job failure/latency across the now-3 renderers. *(still OPEN)*
- **DISPOSITION: ✅ PASS.** No BLOCK, no must-fix. xlsx carry RESOLVED; S5 COMPLETE. DPDP-retention + worker-observability carries remain.
